Local News

Overseas Chinese Representatives from Mexico Hosted Guests Yesterday 127

Report on Anti-Chinese Persecution and Request Assistance; Over a Hundred More Refugees Scheduled to Return Home

Representatives of the distressed overseas Chinese from Mexico, Huang Zhulin, Lin Wenli, Lin Huiyao,

etc., in order to thoroughly clarify the truth about anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico to all sectors of society and to request assistance in urging the government to seriously negotiate with Mexico to alleviate the suffering of overseas Chinese in Mexico, specially held a reception for all sectors of society at the Xinxin Restaurant on Nanjing Road yesterday afternoon at 6:00 PM. More than a hundred people attended, including Mayor Wu's representative, Li Dachao, Chairman of the Central Relief Committee, Xu Shiying, Guo Shun from the Local Association, Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Global Overseas Chinese Federation, Peng Canguang, and reporters from Chinese and Western newspapers. The event began with a thank-you speech and report from Chairman Huang Zhu. Afterwards, Li Dachao, Xu Shiying, Lin Kanghou, and Peng Canguang delivered speeches. The event ended around 8:00 PM. The Chairman's thank-you speech and report on the anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico are recorded below:

Chairman's Speech 128

This time, due to the anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico, distressed overseas Chinese were forced

to return home. On the way through Shanghai, we were first rescued by the Global Overseas

Chinese Federation, taking the lead even before the government. We were also greatly publicized

by the Shanghai media, initiating the effort even before the government. Mayor Wu

Tiecheng planned and coordinated the effort, even before the central government. Now, we are grateful for General Chiang Kai-shek's generous donation of ten thousand yuan, leading the way for party and state leaders to contribute. All of these demonstrate a positive impression. On behalf of all the distressed overseas Chinese, I would like to express our most sincere gratitude. Zhulin and others were entrusted by the overseas Chinese forced to return home from Mexico to stay in Shanghai with two important missions: First, to urge the government to negotiate strongly with Mexico to stop the anti-Chinese persecution, in order to protect the lives and property of the overseas Chinese currently in Mexico (referring to those who have not returned home) from being affected by the anti-Chinese persecution and being expelled again. Second, to find ways to provide relief to the four thousand overseas Chinese forced to return home in the motherland, in order to solve their livelihood problems and alleviate their suffering. However, negotiation and relief are major undertakings, and cannot achieve great results without the cooperation and promotion of all parties. Moreover, the representatives have lived abroad for a long time and are new to returning south. We are unfamiliar with the situation in the motherland and difficult to develop without the guidance and support of all sectors. Therefore, we have prepared this banquet today to invite guidance from all sectors and present the truth about the anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico. This is the reason and significance of our gathering. I am grateful that you have not abandoned us and are willing to come, which shows your concern for the distressed overseas Chinese. We are deeply grateful and bow our heads in thanks. However, what are the methods and objectives of our request for negotiation and appeal for relief? I will now elaborate on this to all of you.

Relief Measures 129

Regarding the methods, (1) first establish a Distressed

Overseas Chinese Relief Association in Shanghai to concentrate the spirit and strength of all

the distressed overseas Chinese as a guiding organization for protecting

the interests of the distressed overseas Chinese.

(2) Begin to carry out a general registration of the distressed overseas Chinese, analyzing their technical skills, in order to find ways to resettle them and relieve their suffering. (3) Raise a large sum of money to establish a Chinese Overseas Factory in Shanghai, specifically to accommodate the general distressed overseas Chinese forced to return home from Mexico and who are unemployed, in order to stabilize their lives and prevent them from becoming beggars. (4) All matters related to relief, whether fundraising or distribution, will be handled entirely by the aforementioned Distressed Overseas Chinese Relief Association, in order to achieve effective relief and avoid disputes.

Request to the Government 130

Regarding the objectives, we have five requests to the government: (1)

Donate a considerable amount of money (or 200,000) as the foundation for the Chinese Overseas Factory.

(2) Donate

fifty acres of wasteland near Shanghai as the land for building the aforementioned factory. (3) Allocate other public land for the distressed overseas Chinese to plant or engage in other agriculture. (4) Within the shortest possible time, order the Navy to send several warships to Mexico to demonstrate strength and provide effective protection. (5) Give our distressed overseas Chinese the opportunity and convenience to help ourselves, and do not obstruct our self-help efforts.

Hope from All Sectors 131

We also have five hopes from all sectors: (1) Appreciate the significant sacrifices made by overseas Chinese

for the country and society, and the suffering they have endured from being oppressed by foreign races, and provide material assistance.

(2) Correct the political discrimination against overseas Chinese and the neglect of the distressed overseas Chinese. (3) Support the implementation of the Chinese Overseas Factory with spirit and material resources. Furthermore, yesterday I read in the newspaper that Comrade Chen Shuren, Chairman of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, reported on overseas Chinese affairs at the Central Memorial Week on the 22nd of this month. In his report, he said, "Recently, we have changed our former discriminatory attitude towards overseas Chinese to one of respect." Based on his statement, Chairman Chen has clearly admitted that in the past, there was discrimination against overseas Chinese. This time, the anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico has become increasingly fierce, causing losses of over 40 million yuan to the overseas Chinese in Mexico, which is due to the government's daily neglect of the interests of overseas Chinese and its failure to protect them. The government should bear full responsibility for this. Based on the latter statement, the government has changed to an attitude of respect, and we hope that the government will fulfill its promise to respect overseas Chinese and immediately provide all the distressed overseas Chinese in Mexico with satisfactory guarantees and protection. Then, why would we ask for another grain of rice for relief?

Report on the Events 132

The anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico has lasted for over two years, and many people know the general situation,

but not the truth. This is because the events can only be described by those who have personally experienced them.

The representatives are all distressed overseas Chinese forced to return

home, having suffered personally and been deeply stimulated. We have experienced

difficulties and dangers.

Now, in order to allow the people of our country to fully understand the situation, we will provide a general report on the facts, shedding tears as we present it to our beloved compatriots and all sectors of Shanghai. We hope that benevolent people will pay attention to it.

Motives for the Anti-Chinese Persecution 133

Foreigners residing in Mexico include Americans, Japanese,

Chinese, Germans, British, Russians, Italians,

Spaniards, and others, totaling no less than 300,000

people. Why is Mexico persecuting the Chinese, and why

is it persecuting the Chinese alone? This has value for research. To find the reasons for this, one aspect is the shadow of the world economy, another is the political disputes in Mexico, and another is the lack of protection from our government. The above points are the general causes of this severe anti-Chinese persecution. At that time, unemployed workers in Mexico and politicians who harbored hatred towards overseas Chinese colluded with each other, took the opportunity to vigorously promote the persecution, and supported each other. From propaganda to action, from action to organization, in June 1931, they openly established the Anti-Chinese Party in Mexico City to carry out a substantive anti-Chinese movement. This is the origin and motive of the anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico.

Ineffective Negotiations 134

Since the anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico began, it has lasted for two years.

Although our government has repeatedly negotiated, it has

not taken practical and effective measures to maintain order. May I ask

the government, has it ever sent a warship to protect our

overseas Chinese? No, it has not. Has it ever sent a commissioner to negotiate and comfort our overseas Chinese? Again, no, it has not. The government has not even taken these simplest measures to protect overseas Chinese. As a result, our overseas Chinese in Mexico are being humiliated and have no protection. Not only are they being expelled, but their property is being looted, and they are even being driven back to their country without food or clothing, like beggars. The various tragic situations are too numerous to recount. Our spiritual and material losses in this anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico cannot be said to be due to the government's neglect of the interests of overseas Chinese and its failure to protect them.

Means of Oppression 135

Among the overseas Chinese residing in Mexico, the number

engaged in commerce and agriculture is the largest.

In terms of business, agriculture,

besides Britain and Germany, we rank third.

However, overseas Chinese have never had strong capital. The reason why

they were able to achieve this position is due to their diligence and hard work. If they had received adequate protection from the government, why would the spiritual value that our overseas Chinese earned with their blood and sweat be seized and destroyed by a small country like Mexico (with a total population of only 14 million and a total land, sea, and air force of only 50,000)? Therefore, although there is more than one reason for the anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico this time, it should be known that the main reason is the lack of protection capabilities of our government. The Mexican government and people, from contempt to abuse, from abuse to violence, from violence to expulsion, have progressed step by step, becoming increasingly fierce. From passive to active, from propaganda to implementation, in the beginning, the Mexican government first promulgated the most severe commercial laws to oppress overseas Chinese. Every Chinese store was limited to ten employees, and eight Mexican natives had to be hired. Not only that, the onerous business tax levied on overseas Chinese increased sharply from ten yuan to one hundred yuan. Our government had no way to negotiate, and overseas Chinese had no choice but to sacrifice everything and voluntarily close their businesses. This is in terms of commerce. Then, the Anti-Chinese Party went out to rob and confiscate registration papers (residence permits), arbitrarily detained people, and subjected them to all kinds of humiliation. All of these are the oppressive means of the anti-Chinese persecution in Mexico. Their cruelty and illegality are unprecedented in the world.

Suffering 136

The Anti-Chinese Party in Mexico's treatment of overseas Chinese

is truly cruel and unprecedented in the world. They treat our Chinese people like

cattle and horses. Their harsh methods

are worse than the treatment of prisoners of war in warring countries. They seize

property, violently beat people, and after beating them, transport them by car and abandon them in the mountains. They have nothing to eat for three days, and many die from starvation and cold. Although we were fortunate enough to escape, surviving by the skin of our teeth, there are still over 20,000 people who have not escaped the danger. How can we sit idly by? The tragedy of this situation makes those who hear it sad and those who see it shed tears. It is truly unfortunate to be born as a citizen of the Republic of China and even more unfortunate to reside in the evil Mexico.

Estimated Losses 137

Among the overseas Chinese residing in Mexico, most are engaged in business

and agriculture, and about 30,000

people are directly or indirectly affected by the anti-Chinese persecution.

Among these 30,000 people, each person has at least 2,000 yuan in assets, totaling 60 million yuan (Mexican silver).

The material losses caused by this anti-Chinese persecution should be in the range of 70%. Although there are no accurate statistics, based on mathematical calculations, it should be over 40 million yuan. The spiritual losses have not yet been calculated.

Difficulties of Returning Home 138

Our overseas Chinese in Mexico have suffered all kinds of harsh treatment from the Mexican government

and unreasonable oppression from the Anti-Chinese Party.

It is impossible to do business, and it is also impossible to engage in agriculture. It is even more impossible for laborers to gain a foothold. If they are not

expelled, they will be trapped in a desperate situation, awaiting death. They have no choice but to consider returning south. However, the issue of returning home is also difficult to resolve. After all, travel expenses require money. Without sufficient preparation, how can they make the journey? After being robbed by the Anti-Chinese Party, under environmental oppression, it is extremely difficult to obtain several hundred yuan for return expenses. However, if they do not find a way to resolve the issue urgently, they will either die tragically or become beggars. This is why our overseas Chinese in Mexico risk great danger to sneak into the United States in search of a glimmer of hope. Unfortunately, they are detained by the US government and eventually repatriated home, which is still fortunate. However, after returning to their homeland, they are penniless and have no home to return to. The difficulties of this situation are hard to describe in writing. They are now wandering on the road, in dire need of assistance. We beg the benevolent people of our motherland to sympathize with their plight, generously donate, and do their best to help. The distressed overseas Chinese will be extremely grateful, and the nation will be fortunate.

Five Batches of Distressed Overseas Chinese 139

The Global Overseas Chinese Federation received a telegram from San Francisco yesterday,

stating that another fifth batch of over one hundred and fifty distressed overseas Chinese

is scheduled to return home on the Da Lai Company's President Hoover ship on the 26th of this month.

After receiving the telegram, the federation immediately rented a large house near the association

to serve as a temporary shelter. When the distressed overseas Chinese arrive in Shanghai, the federation plans to send personnel to the pier to take care of everything.

Coal Shortage in Shanghai 140

Beipiao and Tangshan Fall

Source Gradually Depleted

Telegraph to Other Coal Mines

To Expedite Shipment of Domestic Coal to Provide Relief

Xinsheng News reports that bituminous coal is the most important fuel. Factories, ships, trains, and other fuels cannot do without it. Since the outbreak of military affairs in North China, both the Kailuan and Beipiao coal mines have been occupied by enemy troops, disrupting freight transportation and causing a shortage of supplies. There is a panic in Shanghai's bituminous coal market. A Xinsheng News reporter visited the committee members of the Coal Industry Association yesterday. According to reports, this port has a large sales volume of bituminous coal. Kailuan household-grade sieved lumps, Kailuan No. 2 sieved lumps, Kailuan No. 1 fines, Kailuan No. 2 fines, and Kailuan special fines are the most popular. Datong Grade 2 Carbon sieved lumps, Datong raw coal sieved lumps, Datong raw coal, Datong fines, and Datong Screenings, and Zhongxing sieved lumps and Zhongxing coal fines are also popular. Changxing sieved lumps, Changxing fines, Jingxing sieved lumps, Jingxing fines, Liuhegou sieved lumps, Liuhegou fines, Huadong sieved lumps, Huadong fines, Huadong raw coal, Boshan Xiaoshan sieved lumps, Boshan sieved lumps, Beipiao sieved lumps, Beipiao fines, Nangshan sieved lumps, and Hongshan fines are also relatively popular. However, Beipiao coal has been temporarily stopped from being shipped to Shanghai due to the impact of the Japanese military occupation. Although Kailuan coal has also been affected, it is still possible to ship it to Shanghai because it is managed by a Sino-British joint venture with a British flag, but the number has decreased. Other coals are being shipped to Shanghai as usual. Moreover, with the imminent ceasefire between China and Japan, transportation will soon be restored, so there is no major shortage of bituminous coal in this city.

Dalu News reports that after the reporter extensively inquired about the coal industry situation in this port yesterday,

he received alarming news that the industry in this port may be greatly hindered soon due to a lack of fuel. According to reliable sources, the coal reserves in this port are now insufficient for one month's use. Normally, there are reserves for two or three months. The reason for this is that the Kailuan Mining Bureau, the main supplier of this port, has temporarily stopped shipping coal. The reporter visited people from Kailuan yesterday. They neither denied nor confirmed the claim of temporarily stopping shipping coal, only saying that the news that can be provided to newspapers must be issued by the Northern General Bureau. According to the news received here, the bureau's miners have fled when the Japanese army advanced to Tangshan, causing production and transportation to be suspended. Regardless of whether this news is reliable or not, the shortage of coal reserves in this port is a definite fact. Yesterday, it was heard that leaders of the industry in this port telegraphed domestic coal mines to expedite shipments to provide relief. The coal mine workers have also agreed to do their best to ensure that coal produced in Shandong and Henan provinces will flow continuously to Shanghai. Even the bankers of this port have agreed to provide financial assistance to facilitate the production and transportation of various mines. According to coal merchants, the amount of Shandong coal and Henan coal coming to Shanghai has greatly increased in recent weeks. However, Henan coal must be transported by the Pinghan Railway to Hankou and then loaded onto ships to Shanghai. Recently, the Pinghan Railway has encountered new difficulties in transportation due to military transport. Shandong coal is transported by the Jinpu Railway, but the cost is too high and the transportation is more difficult. It is now heard that Zhongxing plans to lay 30 miles of railway to connect the Longhai Railway so that it can reach Haizhou from the Longhai Line and then be transported by ship to Shanghai, greatly reducing transportation costs. It is also heard that Zhongxing authorities are consulting with leaders of the financial industry to raise funds, and they have also obtained their consent. Although it will take time for this new development to be completed, it is believed that it can be realized in the short term to alleviate the coal shortage in Shanghai.

Rural Economic Relief 141

Banking Association to Hold Meeting This Week to Discuss

The Executive Yuan convened a meeting of the Rural Revival Committee in Beijing on the 5th and

6th of this month to determine the general outline of the measures, and requested the Shanghai Banking Association to establish a Rural Financial Adjustment Committee. The Banking Association is scheduled to

convene a meeting of the Executive Committee this week

to discuss matters related to the establishment of the Rural Financial Adjustment Committee. Yesterday morning, a Central News Agency reporter learned from the banking sector that the opinions of the banking sector in this city regarding rural financial adjustment are as follows:

Concentrate Efforts 142

The banking sector in this city believes that the decline of rural

finance has a great impact on the financial security of the entire country,

and it is imperative to find ways to provide relief. Therefore, the banking sector in this city generally advocates concentrating efforts to carry out the relief, that is, concentrating the efforts of various banks on the Rural Financial Adjustment Committee, which will be responsible for the relief and adjustment matters. However, they fear that the committee will be unable to reach everyone, and the beneficiaries will only be near Shanghai and will not be able to reach all regions.

Conducting Separately 143

There is another group of bankers who advocate that after the establishment of the Agricultural Finance Adjustment Committee, the committee should formulate adjustment measures and separately request each bank to handle matters in various rural areas. For example, Bank A handles matters in area A, and Bank B handles matters in area B. All major banks have branches in various locations and automatically conduct operations by district. The speed of effectiveness is better than the method described in the previous paragraph. However, the disadvantage is that there are concerns about ineffective implementation. The above two opinions will be submitted for discussion at the executive committee meeting.

Farmer Loan Capital 144

As for banks pooling funds to establish farmer loan capital institutions in various rural areas to provide loans to farmers during the lean season, the idea is good. However, it would be unacceptable if those in charge do not understand the purpose of establishing such institutions and instead engage in exploitation. Therefore, the banking community in this city should pay full attention to the preparation of farmer loan capital institutions to avoid such abuses, so as not to lose the original purpose of agricultural finance adjustment and to provide convenience to farmers.

International Trade Bureau Introduces Domestic Product Exports 145

Can be contacted at any time at the Bureau

Manganese powder has a wide range of uses in industry, such as in the production of gas-smelling bleaching powder and disinfectants. It is also needed in considerable quantities in dyeing factories, enamel factories, glass factories, paint factories, and battery factories. Banking Sector Seeks to Rescue Chinese Yarn 146

Three banks will give cash for goods. The government should provide fundamental relief.

Chinese yarn factories are experiencing operational difficulties, leading to reductions in working hours.

The Chinese yarn industry is in a precarious situation. The reasons for its decline have been thoroughly discussed by experts. Recently, the Ministry of Industry, in order to provide relief, will be in contact with national banks to provide loans. According to the banking sector, the revival of the Chinese yarn industry should be resolved by the government through political means. The details are as follows:

Bank Relief 147

It is reported that Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry, recently discussed the issue of rescuing Chinese yarn with Kong Xiangxi, Governor of the Central Bank, and agreed that the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications would provide loans of 20 million yuan, with an annual interest rate of 6%. The Central Bank would be responsible for 4%, and the yarn industry would be responsible for 2%, in order to reduce the burden on the yarn industry and facilitate financial circulation.

Fundamental Solution 148

According to the banking sector, Chinese banks fundamentally always lend to the yarn industry. Shanghai Bank alone has lent around 20 million, resulting in a situation where the bank's cash has turned into cotton yarn. However, this is not a fundamental solution. If a fundamental rescue of Chinese yarn is desired, the responsibility still lies with the government. The government should abolish all harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies when purchasing raw materials, and then take steps to reduce the cost of the yarn industry through protective tariffs, thereby invisibly raising the status of Chinese yarn, which may be helpful.

Westerner Ike Fu Elaborates on Aviation Patriotic Awards 150

Forty Years in China Leads to Love for China, Integrity, Value, and Fair Estimation are Welcome

Mr. Ike Fu, a Westerner, out of sympathy for China's national crisis, donated his real estate and antiques to establish aviation patriotic awards, which has aroused social discussion on its methods. It is now heard that Mr. Ike sent another letter to the preparatory office of aviation patriotic awards yesterday, elaborating on everything. The letter said, "To the gentlemen of the preparatory office of aviation patriotic awards: On the evening of the 18th, I was honored to be visited by leaders from all walks of life in Shanghai, despite their contempt for me. I have received great speeches from you and many compliments from various newspapers. How can I not say a word? I am sixty years old and have been in China for nearly forty years. I have a friendship with the same state and a sense of respect for the official hat. I have often discussed the depth of China's national crisis with Chinese friends and sought ways to deal with it. Later, with the personal guidance of Mayor Wu and the back-and-forth correspondence of representatives of various groups, this plan to use real estate and antiques as prizes was formed. How to initiate, how to allocate prizes, and how to provide aviation patriotic funds are all decided by you. I have absolutely no preconceived notions. I only know that I will contribute my blood, sweat, and hard work to the best of my ability. As for its quality and value, I welcome knowledgeable people to make a fair assessment, and I will not hesitate to estimate it in any way. However, I do not want to hear public insults such as deception based on ignorance of the truth and stubborn subjectivity. If it is said to be promotion, I have already stated it in a special letter. In this serious time, with the patriotic enthusiasm of the Chinese people and the deep sympathy of foreigners living in China, the number must be considerable. I have already begun to plan the promotion method, and I believe that I will not lag behind others. If the sales cannot be smooth, why can't I make reasonable sacrifices based on the actual agreement? As for large military supplies and airplanes, I have repeatedly stated that I will donate them, and I will always adhere to my original intention no matter what. This can be reported to you. Destroying the family to relieve the country's difficulties is a beautiful story in history. However, in my shallow opinion, the people who eat the country's food and live on the country's land have this obligation when they encounter national difficulties. There is no such thing as a good name, and I don't know what kind of reality there is. Now, because of my love for China, unexpected praise and fault-finding have come one after another. This is really beyond what my foolishness dares to speculate. I offer my heart and speak to the best of my ability. I wish you peace. Ike Fu respectfully bows."

Five Batches of Antiques Unloaded Yesterday, Not Yet Completed 152

Only over Three Thousand Five Hundred Boxes Transported, Remaining Scheduled to Continue This Morning

Concession Factory Inspection Issue, Shanghai Concession Authorities to Begin Negotiations 153

Shang Zhen's Representative Cheng Qilu Speaks 154

Cheng Qilu, representative of Shang Zhen, Commander-in-Chief of the Second Army Corps of North China, returned to Beijing from Shanghai last month and rushed to the front to discuss important matters with Shang. Later, Commander-in-Chief Shang believed that the military situation of resisting Japan in North China needed to be reported to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and sent Cheng to Nanchang to meet Chiang and report on the army's anti-Japanese combat experience and request instructions. The details have been repeatedly recorded in previous reports. Now that Cheng has arrived in Shanghai, a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Cheng at his residence. According to him, "I left Beiping on the 29th of last month. At that time, in addition to the fierce fighting that continued for days in the Gubeikou area, the Japanese army in other passes and the Ledong area had been withdrawing continuously since the 23rd of last month. At that time, it was speculated that the reason for their withdrawal was to concentrate their forces to the rear, attempting to pursue and spy on our Sanhe Miyun from the Xinglong area to threaten Pingjin. Therefore, the Military Council transferred our army from the Ledong area to the Tongzhou Sanhe Pinggu area. Because our army had suffered heavy losses after repeated battles and urgently needed to be replenished, we controlled that area. The enemy did not invade. We vowed to fight to the death. Looking back, since our army was ordered to go to Ledong at the end of last year and fought at Lengkou, it has been five months and more than ten fierce battles. The details of the process have been recorded in many Chinese and foreign newspapers. In particular, the Osaka Asahi Shimbun and the Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun and other newspapers in the enemy's country paid special attention to the Lengkou campaign and published it in great detail, so there is no need to repeat it. In this campaign, the enemy used new-style weapons, and we relied on the spirit of sacrifice to fight steel with flesh and blood. The losses had already been taken into account. However, comparing the casualties of both sides, the enemy may have exceeded ours. According to statistics, the casualties of the Huang Gao Division and the Huang Division, which were fighting on the front line, were about two-fifths and one-third, respectively. On average, more officers were killed, because many officers committed suicide in anger after being injured. Reports said that although the initial ceasefire was said to be about to be realized, if the Japanese side put forward excessive conditions, forcing us to form an alliance under the city, our side would not yield, and how could the Japanese side get what they wanted? If unfortunately the peace talks cannot succeed, there is no other way but to defend Pingjin to the death and implement the determination to fight with our backs to the city. At this time of national crisis and people's suffering, when survival is at stake, the fundamental plan is still for the whole country to be of one mind and work together to open up a way out, so that we can overcome this difficulty and save the crisis." According to Cheng, "The Jiangxi communist bandits were quite rampant in the past. Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek personally supervised the suppression, the bandit forces have been greatly reduced. The method of suppressing bandits must be to encircle and suppress with military force, and at the same time, pay attention to political methods to seek fundamental eradication."

City Chamber of Commerce Commends Copper, Iron, and Machinery Industries for Discovering Japanese Iron 155

A Stern Warning Sent to the Iron Industry Association

The City Chamber of Commerce, based on the report from the Copper, Iron, and Machinery Industries Association that Japanese iron was being dumped in Shanghai, sent personnel to secretly investigate. As a result, 600 tons have been discovered. Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce sent a letter of commendation and a stern warning to the Iron Industry Association. The two letters are recorded separately below:

Commendation to Machinery Industry: Received a letter stating that Japanese iron 156

is being dumped in Shanghai. After investigating various factories, more than 600 tons have been discovered. The iron has been strictly sealed and transported to a suitable location to await processing. Your association's public investigation and handling of factories privately importing Japanese iron is consistent with your words and deeds, and you have set a good example. We are very impressed and gratified. In addition to sending another letter to the Iron Industry Association, instructing them to cooperate in investigating and blocking the source, we are writing to inform you first. To the Shanghai City Copper, Iron, and Machinery Industries Association.

Warning to the Iron Industry: We received a letter from the Copper, Iron, and Machinery Industries Association on the 23rd of this month, stating that 157

it received a letter from your association on September 27 of last year, ordering each industry association to establish a branch of the National Goods Promotion Committee. The association immediately began preparations. However, recently, enemy iron has been dumped in this port, and the value of each ton has fallen by more than 20 yuan. Some colleagues have been bewitched and have privately imported it from time to time. Therefore, personnel were sent to various factories for strict investigation. As a result, about 600 tons of enemy iron have been discovered and sealed up. It is planned to transport them to a suitable location to await processing. We would like to know if this is appropriate, and we hope to get your instructions. However, the sale of this kind of enemy iron must go through iron merchants. If you do not investigate the source, but only focus on the end, it is not a fundamental way to block the source. For this reason, we are writing to ask you to order the Iron Industry Association to thoroughly investigate and assist together, and instruct them to give a concrete answer to clarify the situation. We find that the Japanese are making repeated efforts to plot against our Pingjin, but the five-minute enthusiasm of the Chinese people seems to have passed. You, as leaders of the group, are also asked to work hard to move forward to fulfill the long-standing reputation of our nation, which is our best prayer. We received a letter from the meeting stating that the economic severance with Japan was decided at the extraordinary member representatives' meeting in September 20th. Two years have passed since then. Why is it that even now, your colleagues are still selling Japanese iron to machinery factories? It is likely that you have forgotten and have not earnestly followed the order. You are one of the industry leaders of the association, and you are also a member of this association. You have the responsibility to fulfill the resolutions of the general meeting and to earnestly investigate at any time. Since this matter has been publicly investigated and truthfully reported by the Machinery Industry Association, it concerns the rescue of the national crisis. Your association should have the determination to do what is right and not let the association be beautiful in front of you. You must immediately and thoroughly investigate your colleagues and give strict warnings. You should also report the results of the investigation to be reviewed. This is very important. To the Iron Industry Association.

The case has been ongoing for nearly three years, and the impoverished and helpless creditors have only received 20% from the former French Concession court. Moreover, since the case was taken over by your court, it has already been two years, and not a single cent has been repaid. The petitioners are in urgent need of funds as the abolished lunar Dragon Boat Festival approaches, yet Huang Chu Jiu's real estate has not been auctioned. Furthermore, it has been found that all of Huang's real estate is mortgaged to others. The only hope for the petitioners, as ordinary creditors, is the remaining amount after the auction proceeds are used to repay the mortgages. And the sooner the remaining amount is repaid, the more it depends on when your court holds the auction. The petitioners, being in urgent need of funds, have repeatedly submitted petitions urging the auction, but your court has not actively carried out the auction. Therefore, they are submitting another petition, earnestly requesting that you consider the extreme poverty of the petitioners and expedite the auction as soon as possible, so that the savings can be repaid at an early date.

Page 11

Measures to Reduce Silk Cocoon Freight Rates on Two Railways

Silk Cocoon Groups Notify Members that Prices Set are Cheaper than Shipping

Cocoon merchants in various parts of Zhejiang have now started weighing cocoons, and the prices set are 27 yuan per dan for top grade and 25 yuan per dan for second grade. Yesterday, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Huitong Transportation Company loaded the first batch of spring cocoons at the Chang'an Station, totaling 138 packages. They were transported to the South Station for unloading. They were purchased by the Chang'an Xinshun Cocoon Firm and delivered to the Shanghai Fuchang Silk Factory. It is reported that most of this year's spring cocoons are produced from improved silkworm breeds, with large and firm cocoons. However, due to the harvest in various places, the overall yield is only half, mainly due to the cold weather, which has reduced the harvest. Due to cost considerations and low market prices, silkworm farmers are temporarily unwilling to sell easily and are waiting for prices to rise. Therefore, although various cocoon firms have started weighing and buying, there is no crowding. The railway authorities, in order to protect cocoon merchants and increase transportation business, have specially reduced the freight rates for these goods, changing the calculation of freight charges to third-class goods, which were originally calculated as second-class goods. Therefore, most of this year's cocoon transport is by train to Shanghai.

The decline of the silk cocoon industry in recent years has reached an extreme point. The size of the freight rate is closely related to the cost of raw silk. Therefore, representatives of the silk industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang have repeatedly requested the Ministry of Railways and the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus to reduce freight rates in order to maintain the industry. Director Yu of the Ministry of Railways and the directors of the two railway bureaus all recognized that Chinese silk is an important part of foreign trade and that in this economic downturn, it is appropriate to reduce freight rates to assist the development of the silk cocoon industry and benefit transportation by reducing costs. Yesterday, the Ministry issued an approval to charge according to the third-class freight rate, which is cheaper than shipping. For example, loading at the Zha Kou Gate and being responsible for transporting to the North Station, including loading and unloading fees and delivering by car to the foreign firm or silk factory, the standard is 48.8 cents per package of 40 Jin (Chinese pound) . Gongchen Bridge is 47.3 cents per package, Chang'an is 43.1 cents per package, Xieqiao is 42.5 cents per package, and Jiaxing is 36.3 cents per package. The same applies to the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway. The freight rate from the starting station to Shanghai, including delivery to the foreign firm or silk factory, is 51.5 cents per package from Nanjing, 44.8 cents per package from Zhenjiang, 37.2 cents per package from Changzhou, and 32.9 cents per package from Wuxi. This is based on a standard weight of 40 Jin per package. If shipping from Wuxi, as in the past when each package only weighed 36 Jin, then each package is only 30.4 cents. The above-mentioned responsible delivery method was negotiated and implemented by silk industry leaders and the railway bureau, so that silk merchants in the interior can directly report to the station for loading after completing the cocoon collection, which can avoid the losses caused by the lack of vehicles and waiting for cars, and can also save the various procedures such as sending friends to pick up goods at the South Railway Station. Therefore, since the implementation of the new regulations, all stations on the two railways are preparing empty cars to wait, in order to achieve the purpose of loading as soon as possible, and it is stipulated that all goods will be transported to the Shanghai North Railway Station, and after unloading, they will be directly moved onto the car and sent directly to the foreign firm or silk factory according to the instructions of the cocoon merchant at the time of loading, to complete the procedures. If there is theft in transit, the railway bureau is responsible for compensation. Therefore, when loading the car, the cocoon packages must be weighed one by one and handed over to the stationmaster to clarify the responsibility. The above methods are being notified to the members of the Shanghai and Wuxi Silk Factory Trade Unions and the Zhejiang Cocoon Industry Federation for their reference. It is also learned that the railway bureau is publishing the freight rates in the newspaper to inform the public.

Customs Regulations on Merchant Ship Steering Gear Orders 178

Shipowners Should Be Aware

The Jianghai Customs Tax Commissioner issued a notice yesterday, stating that in order to announce matters, the government has ordered that all Chinese merchant ship steering gear orders (i.e., emergency driving command orders used to communicate with the helmsman) should be implemented with direct meaning from May of this year. For example, when the ship is moving forward and the rudder wheel and bow are to turn to the right, the English word RIGHT should be used to command it. Conversely, if the rudder wheel and bow are to turn to the left, the English word LEFT should be used to command it. As for ships using manual steering, the command orders used must also be implemented uniformly, that is, RIGHT means commanding the rudder blade and bow to the right, LEFT means commanding the rudder blade and bow to the left, etc. Therefore, all shipowners should be aware of this, and this notice is hereby issued.

Regularly Maritime Pirates Loot Fishing Boats 179

The Yongbo Fishing Association Petitioned to Send Warships to Pursue and Arrest

The Jiangzhe Industry Improvement Association and the Jiangzhe District Fisheries Administration in this city

Yesterday, according to the Yinxian Fishing Association's petition, member Zheng Gensheng reported that when the people went fishing at sea, they hired four large pairs of ships. On the 17th of this month, they were transported to Xiaobanshan in Dinghai County (after unloading the goods, they were preparing to turn back the empty ships when a pirate ship passed by. Eight bandits, each holding a handgun, looted several empty ships. One ship was released, stating that each ship would cost 120 yuan, and the money would be paid off within five days. Otherwise, the three ships will be confiscated, etc., so I urgently reported to the meeting. In the fishing season, the livelihood of the fishing industry depends on the proceeds at this time to live on, but in this era of piracy, looting is repeated. Fishermen go out to sea to fish, and they are deeply worried, anxious, and trembling. I hope that our government will give them real protection, ensure water security, and make them feel at ease and happy, and engage in production. Then the news came, and it turned out to be the opposite. My fishermen's hope will be lost from now on. Recently, the government has collected a fishing industry construction fee, which is not a small amount. One is to purchase patrol ships to protect fishermen, and the other is to take it from fishing and use it for fishing. However, what we see and hear is that fishing boats are being robbed and fishermen are being looted, which is still the case. Therefore, there is a reason why the number of fishing boats has been sharply reduced and the fishing industry has declined this year. If we do not seek remedies quickly and try to recover, our country's fishing industry will be reduced to a place of no recovery and will never be revived. According to the previous situation reported, it is reasonable to prepare a document and submit it to the authorities to order their subordinates to send warships to pursue and arrest in order to protect fishermen and eliminate piracy, etc. After receiving the report, the association and bureau ordered the warships to protect them separately, and also sent a letter to the Outer Sea Water Police Branch to instruct each team to assist.

Yangzhou Association Discusses the Gao Case 180

丨Eight Resolutions on Important Matters丨

The Shanghai Yangzhou Eight Counties Association of fellow villagers, located in Renji Lane, Xinzha Road, invited representatives from local groups and committee members to a meeting at 3 PM yesterday to discuss the direction of negotiations regarding the Gao case. More than 40 representatives from various circles attended. Shen Dingchen, the representative of the association, was elected as chairman and reported on the purpose of the meeting. Then, Song Shixiang reported that after receiving the request letter from Gao Yuanlin, the father of the deceased Gao, the association had previously discussed providing assistance and requested the court for a re-examination through lawyers, which was not approved. However, a copy of the court's autopsy report had been received and should be studied first. Next, Committee Member Jian Shusheng said that according to the court's inspection, it was initially said that there were no injuries, but after the second internal autopsy, there was blood in the lung cavity, which was therefore identified as lung disease, but the lower part of the injured area was not examined, so further research was still needed. Next, Committee Member Jiao Chen reported on the petition to the municipal government, which was very successful. Then, the chairman reported that lawyer Zhu Gaorong, a fellow villager, had sent a letter expressing his willingness to participate in the assistance. Next, Mr. Tang, the representative of the barbers' association, reported on his views on the Gao case negotiations. Subsequently, representatives from various groups, such as Chen Guoliang and Yi Lizhang, successively expressed their opinions on the handling of the Gao case. After full discussion, the following decisions were made: (1) The court's appraisal report will be sent to the medical association and fellow villager Dr. Lu for detailed study, and then a protest will be filed with the court. (2) An Aid Gao Yatou Tragedy Support Association of all circles in Shanghai will be organized, and each group and fellow villagers' association will be invited to nominate one or two responsible representatives to participate in the meeting. (3) Collect evidence after the Gao case occurred in preparation for filing a protest with the court, and ask the municipal government to negotiate seriously based on the facts. (4) Establish a legal research association, scheduled to invite lawyers to participate in discussions on May 26. (5) Summon witnesses to truthfully prove the circumstances of the matter. (6) Request newspapers to publicize the news of the Gao case negotiations as much as possible, and regularly invite journalists to hold a tea party, the date to be determined by the association. (7) Jointly seal and submit a public letter to the municipal government and diplomatic organs by major groups to negotiate with the French authorities. (8) Distribute the court's appraisal report to all circles for research and solicit opinions. All the above cases were unanimously approved for execution. Finally, Mr. Lu, the representative of the Quanzhang Middle School teachers and students association, reported on the destruction of the school by the school board, the case was serious, and requested assistance. The meeting adjourned around 5 PM after the discussion.

Zhang Desheng, a Shandong foreman in the tobacco leaf room of the Nanyang Tobacco Factory, because

Jiading Association Sends Letter to the Ratepayers' Association Regarding the Lu Yuanquan Case 182

丨Request a Reasonable Negotiation, Punishment of the Murderer, and Compensation丨

The Shanghai Jiading Association of fellow villagers, regarding the tragic death of Jiading native Lu Yuanquan, who was shot and killed by Italian Marine Corps trainees practicing shooting on the morning of the 23rd of this month, immediately sent a letter to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association requesting a reasonable negotiation to achieve the purpose of punishing the murderer and providing compensation after sending personnel to investigate. The letter from the association to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association is recorded as follows: We are writing to inform you that at about 10 AM on the morning of the 23rd, the Italian Marine Corps stationed in Shanghai was practicing shooting near the target range at the end of North Sichuan Road. Our fellow villager Lu Yuanquan, 42 years old, was engaged in flower planting on rented land at No. 2 Xitiyu Road, Jiangwan Road. At that time, he was inspecting the flower beds when a bullet suddenly flew in and shot in from his forehead, piercing through the back of his head, and he died instantly. After our association learned of this, we immediately sent people to investigate and learned that Lu Yuanquan's family had no permanent property, and his funeral arrangements were desolate. He has an elderly mother above and a wife below, and several members of his family will be left without support from now on. This unexpected tragic death is truly pitiful. Although it is said that the Italian Marine Corps did not intentionally kill him, shooting also has regulations, and the flower beds are not targets. Disregarding human life is a deserving crime, and compensation for the orphaned should be generous. Therefore, we are writing to request your association to negotiate reasonably: (1) Punish the Italian soldier who accidentally injured Lu Yuanquan. (2) Provide generous compensation to Lu Yuanquan's family. We believe that your association has always upheld justice and will do its best to carry out this task and speak out against this injustice for the innocent civilians who died tragically. Sincerely yours, to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association.

With endless friendship, to the editor of the Shen Bao Newspaper, the Shanghai Branch of the China Seamen's Industrial United General Association Organizing Committee. To the esteemed Mr. Editor: Yesterday, I read in your newspaper a report on a brawl among coolies at the Lantai Chimney Pier in Pudong, which mentioned a gang led by Zhu Zuoshu, a coal-carrying coolie from the Kaiping Bureau. After investigation, there is no such person as Zhu Zuoshu among the workers managing the Kaiping Bureau pier. Only I am named Zhu Zhushu, and I have served at the pier for many years and have never heard of anything external. That morning, I went to a friend's place in Puxi to reciprocate, and returned only at midnight, which is known to my colleagues. I am deeply afraid of confusion and damage to my personal reputation, so I specially write this letter to you, and ask the editor to be especially considerate and make a correction. Zhu Zhushu, May 24th.

We are writing to inform you that on the 21st of this month, we read in your newspaper an article about a visit to the First Special District Women's Prison, which stated that "although the number of prisoners is increasing day by day, the prison food is still the fixed quota of one hundred and several tens of mouths in the past, so it is quite difficult to allocate it." After investigation, the prison food item of our prison originally budgeted for 170 people. If the number of prisoners exceeds this, the extra food expenses have always been applied for according to the number of people, and there is no difficulty in allocating it. We should request a correction accordingly. Sincerely yours, the Jiangsu Second Prison Branch, May 24th.

We cannot but believe that the rumors are mistaken. We have asked them to send personnel to assess the damage suffered by the John Cudworth vessel, and our company will demand compensation from the owner of the He'an vessel for this damage. We should ask your newspaper to correct the previous record and publish the enclosed two letters in the same way. We are grateful for this. Da Feng Company, May 24th. We also know that your company's vessel should be fully responsible for the collision, so we specially write to request that you bear all losses and the consequences of the collision. (Enclosed Letter 2) "May 22nd, Da Feng to He Tai" We are writing to inform you that regarding the sections mentioned in the last paragraph of your letter of May 20th, our company firmly denies any liability of any kind mentioned therein, and requests that your company bear all losses and consequences arising from the collision between the John Cudworth and He'an vessels, because this collision was entirely due to the error in navigation of your vessel. Reader Advisory

A Broken Family 193

丨Letter from Mr. Tian Chongshi of Yichang丨

I see many difficult questions in your column, and you answer them all. I also have many things now, please give me detailed instructions. I am now eighteen years old. In the past seven years, life was quite good. My father was a businessman and sent me to a private school for three or four years. Later, due to the sluggish market, there was no business, and my father became addicted to opium and various other habits, deteriorating day by day, turning a happy family into a place where "there is no rice for the chickens by day, and no rats steal food at night!" My father, affected by economic hardship, had no choice but to go out to seek a living. He abandoned my mother, me, my younger sister, and brother. My mother sold all the things in the house to survive! Hoping that my father would send money back, but he never sent a penny home in two years. My mother thought there was no way to make a living, let alone money for my studies, so she asked someone to introduce me to an apprenticeship. Later, my uncle sent me to a machine-made noodle factory to learn the trade, but after entering the shop, there was no business acumen to be seen at all. I was only thirteen years old at the time, with little knowledge, and I didn't refuse. Later, I gradually felt that this kind of business was not clever at all, and even those who had never learned it could do it. I told my mother several times that I didn't want to do it, but my mother said, because of economic difficulties, wouldn't we starve if we went home? So she coaxed me, saying that every profession produces an expert, don't worry, after three years of apprenticeship, you can borrow some money and start your own business. So I slowly continued to work, but my ability to study was gone. I only studied writing and arithmetic during those three years. But the shop owner didn't even subscribe to a newspaper, so my progress in learning was hindered. Seeing that three years had passed, I decided not to do it anymore. Without telling my mother, I quit my job with the shop owner and moved all my bedding back home. At that time, my mother couldn't do anything about it. Soon, my father also came back. My mother tried to help him find a way to do business, and as a result, he opened an opium den, earning half a dollar a day, which was enough to make a small living. I thought it wouldn't be a long-term solution to stay at home, so I asked someone to introduce me to a general store to work. The general store was a little better than the noodle factory. But the initial wage was very low, only two dollars a month to take home. Saving carefully, it could be used for three days. Now, a ban on opium has suddenly arisen in Yichang, and all opium businesses are not allowed. My father is unwilling to do anything other than run an opium den, and there is no way to pay for living expenses. Even if I take my wages home to use, where will the money for the remaining twenty-seven days come from? My mother is also sick with worry, and the scene of not eating for three days and not lighting a fire for two days has also come. I thought to myself that I don't have any other skills at this time, how can I earn more money? I want to ask the shop owner for more wages, but on the one hand, the boss's business is not good, and on the other hand, I don't have much ability, so how can I deserve more money? I want to do business, but I don't have any capital. If I don't take care of my family, wouldn't the whole family starve to death? If I take care of them, I don't have that much strength. You see how dangerous my future and present are! I have been wanting to write this letter for a long time, and I only wrote it tonight. Please have mercy on me and think of a way for me.

Answer: After reading your letter, we feel really sad. To plan for you, you can only use the wages you earn as living expenses for your mother, and you can ignore your father. We don't need to have any sympathy for opium addicts, they have become a social burden. If your mother has two dollars a month, she can wash clothes for others, or do some needlework, and she won't starve. In the vast sea of people, without solving the fundamental problems of the whole society, there is no other good way for your situation.

Education News Highlights

Depending on Local Conditions

Elementary Schools May Not Hold Joint Examinations 194

(Nanjing, 24th) The Ministry of Education, based on the petitions from the education departments of Hunan, Jiangsu, and other provinces requesting changes to the elementary school joint examination methods, finds them quite reasonable and has approved the changes. Elementary schools may, depending on local conditions, not hold joint examinations.

Zhou Fo-hai, Director of Jiangsu Education Department

Letter to Students Taking the Joint Examination 195

Zhou Fo-hai, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, wrote to the students taking this year's graduation joint examination, saying, "To all third-year vocational students in the province: The academic atmosphere in Jiangsu has always been simple and honest, and the talent and morale are superior to other provinces. You are the lifeblood of the country and the focus of the national spirit. You should understand the difficulties of family burdens and have a long-term view of your personal future. How should you study hard and abide by the law? Recently, I heard that a small number of students have begun to doubt this year's joint examination, either questioning the system itself or the subject matter, or even abandoning their studies, secretly running around, publishing leaflets, and spreading them widely. This not only damages the virtues of young people's hard work but also betrays the original intention of the country's encouragement. The joint examination system is a legacy of Prime Minister Sun's examination ideas and a major policy promulgated by the country. It is intended to promote teaching efficiency, select true talents, and improve culture. This is already well known to you. In all areas where education is developed, it is universally followed, such as Zhejiang, Hunan, Shandong, Anhui, and the two cities of Shanghai and Nanjing. There are only differences in timing, but few cases of defiance. Jiangsu's education is admired throughout the country, how can we willingly lag behind and not be a leader for the country? As for why you doubt the joint examination, some say that the standards are too high and the time is too short. However, the standards for each subject were all formulated by the principals of secondary schools in this province after careful consultation, and the longest subjects were selected from each school to compile them, which were then submitted to this department for review and promulgation. Moreover, the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry have long been the basis for teaching in each school. This department is still worried that they may not be fully suitable for the current situation in Jiangsu, so each school has conducted repeated research and jointly formulated the standards in order to reduce difficulties and make them easier to implement. This cannot be said to be prudent and thorough. Moreover, for all systems, when they are first created, there must be people who are 'loyal and devoted to the law' to break the traditional mentality of 'it is easy to enjoy success, but difficult to plan the beginning.' Young people are the vanguard of the revolution, and scholars are the model for the whole people. If they lack this kind of spirit and courage of 'loyalty and devotion to the law,' they carelessly ignore the country's good laws and intentions, and are suspicious of everything. Those who know may think that your minds are driven by emotions, and that the majority are hijacked by the minority, which leads to their sighing. Those who do not know may directly think that you are afraid of difficulties and seek ease, and are cowardly, like the truancy of students in elementary school, which is ridiculed by those who know. People all over the country, who once praised Jiangsu's education and expected Jiangsu's youth, will soon leave in disappointment. Is this what this department and you want to hear? In the past year or two, perhaps because of the many misfortunes of the country, or because of the special circumstances of each school and place, you have not been able to study with peace of mind. This department is well aware of this pain. However, the joint examination system is a major national policy, and this department strictly abides by the law and is determined to implement it without hesitation or delay. At the same time, the love for you is like a father and brother comforting their children, and we cannot allow indulgence to cause lifelong harm. How can there be any feelings of destroying and hurting flesh and blood? Therefore, for anything that is truly beneficial to you, even if you do not see it, we will do our best to plan it and have more than enough. For anything that is truly harmful to you, even if you all like it, we will do our best to eliminate it and make it thorough. Therefore, for the implementation of this joint examination, we will act according to reason and discretion, and be considerate and comprehensive. We never want to see the country's best system become a thorn in the side of young people, and we especially cannot bear to see pure and lovely young people become meat on the chopping block. If we are not insane, how can we deliberately make things difficult for you and deliberately make the majority of you fail? This is not only unreasonable, but also how can we feel at ease? From junior high school to senior high school, you have worked hard for six long years. Now that graduation is near, how should you cherish this long-term, arduous effort, resolutely participate in the joint examination to complete your achievements and seek advancement? If you stubbornly cling to your prejudices and abandon yourselves, then the Ministry of Education's orders and the provincial government's resolutions are clearly visible. Those who do not participate in the joint examination, although they will not be forced to participate, will definitely not be allowed to graduate. Your years of time will be destroyed in one day, and your parents' full hopes will be in vain. Even if this department wants to do its best to save you, it will not be possible. If there are still those who hold onto the crowd and force others to rebel, then they are a scourge to the community, easily breeding problems, destroying laws and disciplines, and disrupting order. National laws and decrees will never be lenient. Where to go and what to do, you should be especially vigilant. I hope you will deeply reflect, concentrate on studying, and prepare for the exam. In the past, when Ran Qiu helped Ji, Confucius, after much regret, said that the young men should beat the drums and attack him. Before Zhou Chu killed the dragon, who knew that he had the courage to change his ways and strengthen himself? I urge you to strive for this. I sincerely tell you, please be aware of it."

(Beiping, 24th) The books and woodenware of the Institute of History and Philology of Academia Sinica in Beiping will be moved to Shanghai in the next few days.

Chinese Education Film Association

Decides to Produce Six Educational Films 197

(Nanjing, 24th) The Second Plenary Session of the Executive Committee of the Chinese Education Film Association was held at the Ministry of Education on the 23rd. Chen Lifu, Duan Xipeng, Qian Changzhao, Guo Youshou, Peng Baichuan, Wu Yinyi, and others attended. It was decided to produce six educational films. The topics are: (1) Family hygiene, (2) Student life, (3) Various new constructions, (4) Domestic porcelain industry, (5) Agricultural improvement, (6) Chinese music. In addition, the domestic silent film "Humanity" and the sound film "Flower of Freedom" were each awarded a commendation certificate. A letter of encouragement was sent to Tianyi Company for the sound film "Vitality." Guo Youshou, Chen Lifu, Peng Baichuan, Wu Yinyi, and Chu Minyi were selected as standing committee members.

Beijing Municipal Primary and Secondary Schools

Representatives Arrive in Nanjing to Request Allocation of Subsidies 198

(Nanjing, 24th) The monthly education expenses for primary and secondary schools in Beijing are approximately 80,000 yuan. Previously, 50,000 yuan was allocated from the leap month of Chong, and the rest was raised by the Beijing municipality. Later, due to the abolition of the Chong Customs, the Ministry of Finance was responsible for allocating the funds. The current arrears have reached more than 700,000 yuan. Recently, because the financial situation in Beijing is critical, the schools cannot maintain their operations. Therefore, Wang Liangcai and Feng Liuxi were specially sent as representatives to Nanjing to urge the allocation of subsidies. They left Beijing on the 22nd and arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 24th. They plan to petition the Executive Yuan and the Ministries of Finance and Education on the 25th.

News from the Ministry of Education 199

A summary of recent news from the Ministry of Education for the past two days is as follows: (1) The Ministry of Railways replied that student groups traveling by train should have the president of the school directly send a letter to the traffic department of the route to issue a discount coupon in order to comply with the procedures. (2) Regarding the matter of temporarily using the funds for the Labor University, which the Ministry of Education previously requested, the Executive Yuan has instructed that before the arrears of the Zhejiang mint tax are received, the Ministry of Education is allowed to temporarily use the remaining funds of the Labor University. (3) Regarding the request for a pension for the late employee Yang Gengying of Beijing Normal University, it should be approved. In addition to submitting the request to the Executive Yuan to be forwarded to the National Government for record, the Ministry of Finance will be requested to verify and handle the matter and reply. (4) Instructed Henan University that the school's law and economics departments are allowed to continue to enroll students, with a limit of 20 students each year. (5) Replied to the China Colonial Border Society that the establishment of branches by the society should be handled in accordance with Article 2 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the General Outline of the Organization of Cultural Groups formulated by the Central Government. (6) Consulted the Training Headquarters on the preparation situation for the case of centralized summer military training for public and private colleges and universities in Shanghai. (7) Submitted a report to the Executive Yuan on the Preparatory Committee of the National Games, requesting the approval of the seal and small seal to be used on May 11.

Shanghai Secondary School Association

Boy Scout Review Ceremony 201

▲ More than 1,000 Boy Scouts from 13 Schools Participate

▲ Mayor Wu, Commander Dai, and Others Serve as Reviewing Officers

The Shanghai Secondary School Association held a grand Boy Scout review ceremony for member schools at the Municipal First Public Sports Field in Nanshi yesterday afternoon starting at 2 p.m., and performed wonderful programs. The details are as follows:

▲ Participating Schools The schools participating this time include 13 schools, with a total of 1,505 Boy Scouts. The order of arrangement is as follows: (1) Provincial Shanghai High School, (2) Guanghua Affiliated High School, (3) Guangzhao Public School, (4) Yucai Middle School, (5) Fudan Middle School, (6) Mullen Middle School, (7) Huahua Middle School, (8) Daxia Affiliated High School, (9) Qingxin Middle School, (10) Minli Middle School, (11) Chengzhong Middle School, (12) Jingye Middle School, (13) Pudong Middle School.

▲ Association Staff Chairman Zheng Xigu, Chief Commander Leng Xueqiao, Deputy Commanders Yu Kuiguan and Zhang Xunfang, Layout and Guidance Sun Yixin and Zhao Weizu, Disciplinarian Sun Zhibin, Reception Zhang Zhongbao, Jia Foru, Wei Jiguang, Tian Ding'an, Wu Xianglin, Zhang Shilin, etc.

▲ Review Order Reviewing officers: Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Garrison Commander Dai Ji, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Department Tong Xingbai, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau Wen Hong'en, etc. The order of review is as follows: (1) Order to prepare, (2) Assembly, (3) Music, (4) All stand at attention, (5) Flag raising, (6) Sing the Party Song, (7) Give the highest salute to the Party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (8) The Chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will, (9) Silent tribute, (10) Review, (A) Report the number of people, (B) Separation ceremony, (C) Basic movement exercises, (D) Marching formation, (11) Chairman's speech, (12) Admonition, (13) Speech, (14) Sing the Boy Scout song, (15) Music, (16) Cheers, (17) Photography, (18) Performance, (19) Dismissal.

▲ Mayor's Admonition After the review, Chairman Zheng Xigu gave a speech, followed by Mayor Wu's admonition, which roughly stated: "Today, the Shanghai Boy Scouts are holding a review in front of the citizens of Shanghai. The important significance of this is to constantly review the strength of our citizens. Boy Scouts are our Chinese students, well-trained young people, and future social cadres and national pillars. The responsibility they bear is very great. During your schooling, you are receiving education and increasing your knowledge and abilities, in order to be prepared to shoulder the great responsibility of the country in the future. In the past few decades, because our ancestors did not work hard, or their efforts were ineffective and fruitless, today China is divided and oppressed by the Japanese. Although our military and civilians have always resisted, they still cannot defeat the Japanese. This is entirely because China was not prepared in the past 100 years, which is why we are suffering today. If we are thinking about the future Republic of China, we must cultivate strength now, and this strength is in you. You are like a tree, a flower, a tender flower. The country cultivates you in order to make you grow into pillars, so I hope that you will make great aspirations, make great preparations, and take on the responsibility of saving China in the future. Today, seeing that the Shanghai Boy Scouts have such good training, it is really the hope of China's future. I also hope that you will continue to work hard to exercise your bodies and increase your knowledge, and become good citizens of China in the future."

▲ Dai's Admonition Commander Dai's admonition roughly stated: "I am very happy to be here today to participate. China today is not only getting worse year by year, but almost day by day. The most hopeful for those who bear the responsibility of saving the country are young people, and they need strong and high-spirited young people. Looking at Germany during the European War, after the war, the national armed forces were completely disbanded, but today Germany's position is very important. This is all due to the efforts of the German people. This spirit of hard work is very commendable for us to learn from. Now that the country is in danger, we should not be pessimistic, as long as the people of the whole country can strive for success. I hope that you, the respectable and lovable young people, will take the spirit of the German people as an example, and one day you will be able to avenge yourselves and wipe out the humiliation."

▲ Summary of the Speech Continuing with Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Department Tong Xingbai's speech, roughly stated, "China's position is declining day by day, entirely due to the declining national spirit of China. To save China, we must first save the Chinese national spirit. Boy Scouts are the most trained and organized citizens, with the habits of obeying discipline, following orders, and living in groups, and the virtues of automatically helping others and never slacking off. Therefore, if we want to save China, we must promote this Boy Scout training from schools to society." Finally, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau Pan gave a speech, roughly stating that "Benevolence, wisdom, and courage, and benevolence is the center of Boy Scout training. The Prime Minister said that wisdom is knowing benevolence, and courage is practicing benevolence. The so-called benevolence is 'diligently practicing is close to benevolence.' Diligent practice has two meanings: on the one hand, using all strength to do it, and on the other hand, doing it with strong strength. This spirit can be seen in the Boy Scout area, because Boy Scouts have the spirit of obedience and mutual assistance. The Japanese say that China has no organization, and its problem lies in disobedience and lack of mutual assistance, so if you ask for benevolence, you can practice it by doing things with these two kinds of training."

▲ Performance Programs Finally, the Boy Scouts from each school performed. The programs included: (1) First aid (Shanghai High School), (2) Sign manipulation and hard work in games (Shanghai High School), (3) Exercises (Guangzhao), (4) Chinese martial arts and lion dance (Guangzhao), (5) Flag language (Fudan), (6) Human pyramid (Mullen), (7) Watchtower (Daxia), (8) Rescue (Daxia), (9) Pen stroke flag language and doing one good deed every day (Qingxin), (10) Camping competition (Minli), (11) Military stick stacking Luo Bin (Chengzhong), (12) Harmonica ensemble (Chengzhong), (13) Unpacking and packing (Jingye), (14) Stacking Luo Bin (Jingye), (15) Watchtower (Pudong). In particular, the watchtower of Daxia was the most exciting. The event ended at 6 p.m.

Notice from the Municipal Education Association

Education Associations in Each District Should Re-elect as Soon as Possible 202

▲ Those Who Have Re-elected Should Report as Soon as Possible

The Shanghai Municipal Education Association issued a special notice to each district yesterday regarding the re-election of education associations in each district within a time limit, saying, "Respectfully, it has been decided at the eighth meeting of the board of directors of this association that the education associations in each district must prepare for re-election in accordance with the schedule, and notices have been sent in succession. Now that more time has passed, most of the districts have completed the re-election, but there are also a few districts that have been slow to hold it. In order to ensure that the re-election in each district is completed as soon as possible, so as to promote the association's affairs, we are hereby sending another notice, hoping that the districts that have already been re-elected will promptly report the re-election situation to this association in detail according to the previous notice. Those who have not yet been re-elected should convene a meeting of staff members as soon as possible to proceed with the re-election, and we hope that the staff members will assist the standing committee in jointly handling the matter. If the standing committee is not in Shanghai, or the staff members are scattered and cannot convene a staff meeting, resulting in a failure to prepare for the re-election, we also hope that the staff members in charge will inform this association in writing within one week, so that this association can send personnel to prepare for the re-election separately. This notice is hereby given, and we hope that you will take note and handle it accordingly."

Chinese Education Association to Unite

Various Groups Discuss Ways to Save the Country 203

▲ Preparatory Meeting Held Yesterday

▲ Members Assigned to Contact Each Other

The Shanghai Secondary School Faculty Association recently convened an emergency board meeting to discuss how to respond to the tense situation and the crisis in Tianjin. It was resolved that the association would initiate and convene a joint conference of various groups in the city to save the country, and representatives were appointed to begin preparations. A preparatory meeting was held at 8:00 a.m. yesterday. Wu Zhiqian, Liu Zirun, Wu Baojin, Huang Yan, Liu Ti'ai, Chen Jicheng, Song Binqin, Ma Zhongkai, and others attended. Liu Zirun chaired the meeting, and Wu Baojin recorded the minutes. The following proposals were discussed: (1) Based on the board of directors' resolution that the crisis in Tianjin is urgent, various groups in the city should be contacted to issue a joint statement to promote national attention. It was resolved to pass the proposal, and Liu Zirun was assigned to draft the statement. (2) How should the standards for contacting various groups be determined? It was resolved to base it on occupations, culture, and other powerful formal groups. For the time being, it will be divided into six types: agriculture, industry, commerce, academia, education, and the freelance profession. Pan Yangyao and Liu Zirun were assigned to contact the agricultural sector, Liu Zirun to contact the industrial sector, Wu Zhiqian and Chen Jicheng to contact the commercial sector, Wu Baojin and Ma Zhongkai to contact the academic sector, and Shen Zuru and others to contact the freelance professional groups. (3) Date of the joint conference? It was resolved to be held before June 4th.

The details of the joint examination for enlistees to the Central Military Academy in Shanghai, organized by the Municipal Education and Public Security Bureaus, have been reported in various newspapers.
