Jiaotong University to Continue Holding Summer School 209

Jiaotong University has been running summer schools since the summer of the 17th year of the Republic of China, for the convenience of students of the school and external students, for four sessions, which has been quite effective. Last year, the school decided to suspend the summer school because it needed to make up for the missed classes during the Shanghai Incident during the summer. This year, the organizing committee will continue to organize it and add many courses to meet the needs. It is heard that this year's subjects in the university department are Chinese, English, physics, chemistry, money and banking accounting, economics, commercial mathematics, railway transportation, mechanics, calculus, materials testing, world modern history, statistics, metalworking practice, industrial analysis, and physics and chemistry teaching methods. The subjects in the high school department are Chinese, English, physics, physics experiments, chemistry, algebra, trigonometry, geometry, higher algebra, analytical geometry, world history, world geography, practical commercial bookkeeping, and outline of economics. The school year is scheduled to be from July 3rd to August 31st.

East Asia Physical Education School to Hold Summer Children's Training Class 210

The East Asia Physical Education School of the Lu Wan district of this city has a Boy Scout instructor training class that has already graduated four classes. Furthermore, a short-term class is opened every summer to allow graduates of the school, physical education teachers and Boy Scout instructors from various primary and secondary schools, and those interested in studying Boy Scout education to use their summer vacation to enrich their Boy Scout knowledge. Since its establishment, it has achieved remarkable results. It is learned that the school will continue to run the program this year, and the school opening is scheduled for July 10th. A prospectus is available upon request. Furthermore, to promote Boy Scouts in this city, a free quota has been specially set up, and the Shanghai Education Bureau has been requested to issue a notice to municipal primary and secondary schools to quickly send personnel to study.

Wan Peng, Principal of Zhongshan School in Siam, Returns to China for Observation 211

Wang Yiding, the principal of the Wan Peng Public Zhongshan School in Siam, has worked at the school for seven years and has worked extremely hard in all matters of management and teaching, with outstanding results. He has now been ordered by the school board to return to China to observe education. Mr. Wang arrived in Shanghai a few days ago. After arriving in Shanghai, the Global Overseas Chinese General Association sent a letter to the municipal government, ordering all educational institutions to take note. The municipal government has agreed and replied, scheduling to visit various schools in this city starting tomorrow, and plans to go to various places in Jiangsu and Zhejiang for investigation.

Rural Areas and National Products National Products Forum 224

— Yang Mang

Rural areas have always been accustomed to using national products, but recently, according to reports from various parties, enemy goods have been like mercury leaking on the ground,

Entering without a hole, taking advantage of its dumping policy, using the skills of unscrupulous merchants, they have actually penetrated into the interior and seized the sales of our national products. It is a pity that the recent rural areas have already been declining and dilapidated beyond description. Ordinary farming families have no savings, and their homes are bare, with no food to eat. They can no longer talk about any enjoyment, and they don't even have the purchasing power. The outlet for national products has already felt very difficult, so those who sell enemy goods take advantage of the opportunity of the farmers' poverty, and batch by batch of low-quality and cheap goods are transported to the interior to cater to their psychology and preferences, and the ignorant and powerless farmers willingly become the major customers of enemy goods. Thus, the enemy goods come in like a landslide, as if entering an uninhabited land, and the farmers who have run out of oil are squeezed again by those who sell enemy goods. Poor rural areas, poor farmers, holding a knife to others, bowing their heads and waiting to be cut. I wonder if those who talk about rural revitalization have thought about it? Have you ever seen it? In the stores in the interior that sell enemy goods, ask them why they willingly work for the

Tigers to harm the Chinese people. They all say that every family is like this. If he sells enemy goods and I don't sell enemy goods, watching others make money and losing money ourselves, who would be willing to do it? There is a person who specializes in department store business. He has several cotton cloth shops in the four townships of Shanghai. He said that after January 28th, only four or five months were doing clean public affairs, and there were no enemy goods at all. Later, those in our industry who were greedy for petty profits slowly sold enemy goods. One family sold, and every family sold. Now it has become an open secret. Anyway, no one is interfering, so just do it, smiling and laughing. These bastards cannot be killed enough, and they are all over the place. Shanghai is like this, and the interior is also like this. The ancients said that there is no greater sorrow than the death of the heart. Now the hearts are really like they are all dead. What else is there to talk about? Alas, it's a pity, it's a pity that this year's National Products Year is just a false name, only getting the newspapers excited and the advertisements dazzling. In fact, where is the National Products Year? It is simply the year when enemy goods are the most abundant. It can be said to be enemy goods. Ask the government, the government doesn't dare to ask. Ask the society, the social department is silent. In the past, those dazzling societies and organizations have left too good of a result. They have long been pointed at by thousands of people and died without a disease. Pity, pity, what kind of world is this? What kind of society is this? Only the rural areas have a small way in the absence of a way. That is, there must be a few foolish people in the local area who are willing to diligently implement import inspections and statistics. For example, how many cigarettes are imported in a month? How many pieces of cloth are imported? How many straw hats are imported? How many glasswares are imported? How many glass utensils are imported? How many undershirts and socks are imported? Create accurate statistics, and use the method of consumer cooperation to purchase directly from national products manufacturers in a centralized manner to distribute to the farmers in the whole village. And there must be a legitimate agency to prove it. In this way, if you do it strictly and fairly, I guarantee that enemy goods will not be able to escape. As long as the leaders in various places who are improving the rural areas are willing to make up their minds and spend a lot of effort to do it, there will definitely be good results. Compared with Shanghai and the metropolis, it feels easier to start. I hope comrades who are enthusiastic about the rural areas will try it out.

National Products Talk Promoting National Products and Relieving Rural Areas 225

— Huang Xuanwan

"The biggest source of national products is the countryside, and the biggest outlet for national products is also the countryside." Mr. Pan Yangyao

In the previous issue of this publication, he has thoroughly told us these two sentences. Indeed, national products factories absorb a large amount of raw materials from the countryside, manufacture them into finished products, and then transport them to the countryside to supply their needs. The close relationship between the two, back and forth, should normally be in the same boat and cycle endlessly. However, since the recent deepening of the rural economic decline, the purchasing power is becoming weaker day by day. The serious situation has affected the sales of national products, adding a major obstacle to the future of developing the national products industry. We will not talk about other things for the time being. According to the recent reports from the Jiashu Six Counties National Products Mobile Exhibition and the Songjiang National Products Exhibition, the difference in results is unprecedented in the past exhibitions, which shows that the rural economy is extremely exhausted and accelerating its collapse. The facts are all there and obvious. Therefore, we have lost considerable effectiveness for the current situation of relying solely on the loud and hoarse promotion of mobile sales. There is an urgent need to remedy it with new methods, and we can also get a deep understanding from this. So what will be the trend of our national products factories in the future? How can we remove the thorns in the future and not hinder our scheduled progress? We clearly understand that the withering of the countryside is due to the expansion of the cities. Naturally, we can only assist the financial and industrial circles to try their best to help the countryside, return the production funds used by the countryside, so that they can work hard and increase production. Moreover, developing agriculture is also to reduce the original cost of the national products industry. The pulse is related and cannot be ignored. "Once the countryside gradually has vitality, commerce will naturally be able to revive, and sales can be drastically increased. This important plan to consolidate our own development future is naturally urgent. As for how to formulate a planned and organized plan, we hope that all national products pioneers will 'think long and look back' and conduct in-depth research and implementation.

Tidy Up Local Products 226

— Zhu Shanxiu

Modern so-called national products are disguised foreign goods,

Local products are authentic and genuine national products.

Let's take the smallest one as an example. Everyone

All know about smoking national products cigarettes, but try to see that the import value of cigarette raw materials | tobacco paper | in 1929 was 2,600,000 taels, and in 1931 it was 4,800,000 taels. This is such an astonishing number! Let's calculate it one by one. This sum of money can at least run hundreds of provincial middle schools now. Do you still need to talk about other aspects of clothing, food, housing, and transportation? Alas! Dear compatriots, wake up! To prevent profits from flowing out, the only way is to use local products. Using local products is our bounden duty, it is our self-help.

Do you all want to refute me? "If all Chinese people use

Use local products, then national products factories will inevitably close down, and tens of millions of workers will lose their jobs? Moreover, there are not enough local products to meet the demand now?" That's right, this is inevitable, but don't worry. Mr. Tai Shuangqiu, an educational doctor from Columbia University and a professor at Henan University, has already thought of a plan for us. We are not opposed to machine industry, nor are we going backwards. We do not want capital to be in the hands of a few people, and we do not want large factories in cities. We want to invest capital in the countryside, to buy machines and set up small factories in the countryside, so that everyone has a sideline and all have shares, and will not be slaves to a few people. We must really and practically tidy up the local products and supply our own needs. In this way, we can save the panic of rural economic bankruptcy.

Compatriots, remember it! Local products are authentic and genuine national products. Go to the countryside to tidy up local products!

National Products Discussion

Primary School National Products Movement 228

— Chen Jingyu

I remember that this publication previously published Mr. Guyuan's "University National Products Movement" article, which vividly and meticulously described the psychology and habits of college students who love to use foreign goods. It can be called an article that targets the bad habits and contributes to national products. However, according to my humble opinion, to rectify the end, we must first treat the root: primary school students are the root of college students, and every college student is made from primary school students; therefore, if we want to correct the wrong psychology and bad habits of college students, we should start with the primary school students in its root period. Therefore, I am not afraid of my shortcomings and imitate Handan, and create a primary school national products movement.

Primary school students who have just entered the school threshold are originally ignorant, without any knowledge to speak of, let alone love for the country. They only know to wear clothes when they have clothes, and use things when they have things. They are absolutely ignorant of the choice of materials. And most of the parents lack the ability to distinguish national products. As long as it is something that their children need, they will rashly purchase it. The source of the goods is not a concern: even knowing that it is a foreign product, or even an inferior product, because of the

Good looks and cheap prices, they will buy it regardless of everything: thus creating today's phenomenon of foreign goods flooding the primary school world. Try to set foot in various primary schools, and the students who use foreign goods are almost everywhere: even the pencils and foreign notebooks used, and the balls and billiard balls played with, are mostly imported products. But the general teachers are all blind, turning a blind eye; in fact, they are not unseen, mostly because the clothes they wear are also foreign goods. They have no patriotic concept themselves, so where can they have the mind to guide students? Therefore, the most chilling thing is that the school flag and uniforms, which are related to the overall appearance of the school, are made of foreign cloth; the school authorities have a disregard for national products in their hearts, so how can they expect their subordinates to reject foreign goods?

The number of primary schools in the country is difficult to count.

; And the number of primary school students in the country is especially as numerous as the sands of the Ganges. These salesmen of foreign goods, as numerous as the sands of the Ganges, have an impact on the future of revitalizing national products, which is no less than that of the more than 100,000 college students in the intellectual class; and the magnitude of their leakage is at least comparable to that of college student consumers, or even exceeds it. This kind of "accumulated mistakes into truth" does not know how to believe in national products

If we do not pay attention to this bad habit and change it, then as Mr. Guyuan said, "It will inevitably lead to all the financial resources of the country being sucked away by foreign merchants." When wealth is exhausted and the people are poor, the country can be expected to perish!

I believe that teachers are role models for students. All teachers in primary schools should set an example by themselves and have the necessity to actually use national products. For students, if foreign goods are found, they should not be afraid of trouble and repeatedly advise them to make them understand and not use them again. And they must always carefully explain the advantages and disadvantages of using national products and foreign goods, so as to cultivate their concept of respecting national products and despising foreign goods; so that they will not repeat the old mistakes of loving to use foreign goods when they go from primary school to middle school to university in the future. Once they step into society and take on the leadership of the masses, the results will naturally be remarkable.

At the beginning of this National Products Year, various places have expressed

Warm support. I think that the principals and teachers of primary schools across the country, who stand in the position of role models for the people, will definitely not lag behind in their patriotic enthusiasm. I sincerely hope that everyone will unite and promote it vigorously, persevere in their determination, and never slacken from beginning to end. The future of national products will be greatly blessed. Work hard! I am looking at it with my neck stretched out.

Industrial Raw Materials Industry Survey Investigation of China's Calcium Carbonate Manufacturing Industry (Part 1) 229

— Songlu

Open a specialized book on the chemical industry, and the first chapter is about the chemical principles of calcium carbonate. Indeed, calcium carbonate occupies a very important position in chemical industrial raw materials, especially in the rubber industry, cosmetics, paper making, sugar refining, paints, and inks; these industries all use calcium carbonate as a primary raw material.

"Promote national goods, resist enemy goods!" This is a national slogan, but the most important condition for the manufacture of a national goods industry lies in the raw material issue. Otherwise, if foreign raw materials are used to manufacture domestic products, the profit rights will still inevitably flow out! What China feels most difficult now is the lack of raw materials. Take calcium carbonate as an example; it is pitiful to say that our country has only had a two-year history of setting up factories for self-production. Before 1931, it could be said that not a single calcium carbonate factory could be found in China! With this kind of so-called resistance to foreign goods, how effective can you expect it to be?

In 1931, Chinese people, recognizing the development of the rubber industry and the lack of domestic raw materials, and also because of the Wanbaoshan Incident, the call to resist Japanese goods was very high. Therefore, people with lofty ideals rose up to plan to establish factories for self-manufacturing. In this year, three calcium carbonate factories were established in Shanghai at the same time: Zhaoxin Chemical Factory, Dachunghua Calcium Factory, and Xinye Chemical Factory. With the simultaneous rise of these three calcium factories in China, the raw material problem of calcium carbonate was fundamentally resolved in our country's industrial manufacturing. Indeed! This is the best record in the industrial history of our country! It is worth introducing to our national goods industrial and commercial circles. Therefore, I will briefly introduce the latest survey of these three calcium factories:

(1) Zhaoxin Chemical Factory: Zhaoxin Factory is located in Chenjiadu, West Shanghai, with a capital of 250,000 yuan. Manager Mr. Li Zuyi graduated from the Mechanical Engineering Department of the University of Hannover in Germany and obtained a master's degree. He is one of the leading talents in mechanical engineering in China. Mr. Li has very detailed experience in mechanical research, so all the machinery in the factory is designed and assembled by Mr. Li himself, and all domestic components are used. This is the most commendable thing about establishing a national goods factory. Chairman Mr. Fang Yexian is one of the most enthusiastic people in the national goods industry. The businesses he runs include China Chemical Industry Company, Jingming Glass Factory, Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Company, and China National Goods Company. Part of the products of the Zhaoxin Factory is supplied to the China Chemical Industry Company as raw materials for manufacturing cosmetics. The factory also has a managing director, Mr. Guo Yongkang, who has also made great contributions to the national goods industry. He has conducted long-term investigations in Japan and has a detailed understanding of the chemical industry in Japan. He has personally investigated the national goods industry in the British, American, and French territories of the South Seas, so he is very familiar with the industrial and commercial situation in the world. The Zupai brand calcium carbonate produced by the factory is manufactured in imitation of the German style and supplemented by the Japanese style. The current daily output is 167 bags (each weighing 100 pounds), with a total weight of 16,700 pounds. In addition to supplying a part of its products to the China Chemical Industry Company for manufacturing cosmetics, the majority is sold to rubber factories all over the country. According to the test results of many chemical experts, the Zhaoxin Factory's products should be recognized as having the lightest quality among domestically produced calcium carbonate (the lighter and purer the calcium carbonate component). The general manager's office for the factory's products is located at Ligong Industrial Raw Materials Company, No. 2500, Henan Road.

Visit Report

A Visit to the Kang Yuan Factory 230

— Yu Qiacheng

I had already recognized the outline of the Kang Yuan Factory in many publications before, and this visit was indeed well-prepared. Although still within the scope of Shanghai, it took quite a while to travel from West Shanghai to East Shanghai. Sitting quietly in the car, I was in a hunting-like contemplation, ready to find some new materials.

This is a miracle! After explaining my intention, I was granted permission. Interestingly, I asked in a roundabout way:

"Could you give me an opportunity today?"

I was not rejected because there was no prior appointment. Mr. Xiang Kangyuan replied straightforwardly:

"Sure, we don't need any preparation!"

Led by two staff members of the factory, I walked through the entire Kang Yuan Factory, including the dormitory, workshop, and sports ground. There were explanations everywhere, especially when I saw the factory motto, that gentleman would explain it eloquently.

The factory roughly includes several parts, from drawing, stone setting, printing, polishing, can making, to packing, like a cycle, going through several procedures in an orderly manner from here to there. There is also a chemical testing department, which is a place dedicated to testing inks. It was working during the visit, but there were only the sounds of machines and iron sheets falling.

Of course, an outsider cannot arbitrarily judge the actual work, but the cleanliness and order of the workshop gave me a very satisfactory impression.

The dormitory is very clean, with bedding of the same color, like the military and schools (in fact, the military and schools in China are not yet like this!). If I hadn't seen it in the Kang Yuan Factory, no one would dare to say it was a workers' dormitory, because the plight of Chinese workers' lives is already an undeniable fact!

The clothes in the storage cabinet are neatly arranged. Although they are all coarse cloth clothes, there are no oil stains or mess. The power of Kang Yuan workers' autonomy can also be proved to exceed the general standard here.

The slogans, creeds, and classrooms of the education department are all like schools. The leading gentleman introduced them one by one, and he could talk about those things like flowing water. It is a pity that it was not during class time, otherwise I would have had to visit the actual factory schooling.

The dining hall is on the second floor, run by the factory itself. In terms of hygiene and worker treatment, this is indeed a great improvement. The sports ground, hospital, and staff residences are all in the factory. According to the Kang Yuan Factory's overview, there are also organizations such as the volunteer army, Boy Scouts, and national martial arts team, and fire protection is also well-known. Unfortunately, I did not have the opportunity to visit those actual worker activities.

This is an idealized factory! Everything is familial and school-like. Although it cannot be said that it can completely solve the suffering of workers, many tasteless troubles have been reduced a lot. However, this is by no means a waste. The excellent quality, honor, and harvest of Kang Yuan products are also sufficient as a reward.

During my visit, there was someone, probably studying labor issues, also visiting there. They raised some questions about the workers, and they all received satisfactory answers.

On a spring afternoon, I walked out of the Kang Yuan Factory alone. Coincidentally, a group of foreign soldiers was conducting field exercises in the open space. Many Chinese people thought it was lively and watched from the sidelines with smiles, without any expression of pain. This really added to my feelings.

Inland Townships and National Goods 231

— Zhou Chenghun

For several weeks, the National Goods Mobile Sales Team has been working hard in many cities, towns, and villages. According to their latest report, two points deserve our urgent attention: one is that the townships around Shanghai are still filled with foreign goods; the second is that the team's banner is everywhere, and the whole town is emptied, and the retail of goods is in short supply.

The first point is the most serious, because in rural gatherings, inland townships with underdeveloped intelligence, letting these foreign goods, enemy goods, flow continuously, makes it impossible for the basic people to see national goods forever. How dangerous and urgently in need of treatment is this? The reason why inland shops have to sell foreign goods and enemy goods is said to be that they also have one-sided difficulties. Because foreign goods have high profits, they have to take care of the lifeline of the shop foundation and the lives of their partners, so they can only quench their thirst with poison and do so. There is absolutely no possibility of selling national goods with extremely low profits. In addition, customers are greedy for cheap prices and love fancy things, and have no time to consider national goods or non-national goods. Therefore, the root of the disease is deeply rooted and it is difficult to change.

If we also use the Shanghai method of issuing warnings and throwing bombs to prohibit unscrupulous merchants from selling foreign goods to inland shops, I dare to assert that the effect will be equally low. The fundamental lies in how national goods factories should diligently reduce costs and lower prices, and how to improve products and strive for favor. Otherwise, squeezing in Shanghai to loudly promote national goods and persuade people to use national goods, while inland is still full of foreign goods, spreading to the countryside, I ask, what is the actual benefit?

The second point seems to be slightly comforting. In fact, the people in the townships are not absolutely fond of foreign goods and enemy goods. Basically, they have not recognized national goods. At the same time, the sale of foreign goods and enemy goods by shops has also covered a layer of curtains between the people and national goods. The national goods exhibitions in major cities in the past lack sincere and universal publicity work, and cannot receive the effect of going deep into the people. All national goods traveling groups with simple organization and short economic means also rush through the market in a hasty manner, leaving no deep impression. I think the National Goods Mobile Sales Team, which is currently working hard, may be able to produce some results.

Because the National Goods Mobile Sales Team has a close relationship with various national goods manufacturers, and the organization and mission are relatively advanced. I think it not only has the task of raising the awareness of national goods among the inland people, but also should use effective methods to assist and guide the inland shops in operating national goods, and eliminate foreign goods in the shortest term!

I am very ashamed to offer the above two points of view to the gentlemen of various national goods factories and the National Goods Mobile Sales Team.

Thus Have I Heard - On Selling Japanese Goods 232

— Ziqiang

The violent sun is approaching, and gods and men are indignant. Pledging to die together, the whole country is in a frenzy. Therefore, economic severance and resistance to Japanese goods have become the most important work at present. However, unscrupulous merchants and market monks sell as usual. The so-called Japanese goods are colorful and fill the market. It is difficult to distinguish between their authenticity and falsehood.

Not only that, but they also establish brand names and cleverly change trademarks, confusing the eye, making it impossible to identify. It is a pity that Yu Ding and Wen Xi cannot discern their treachery. These running dogs of Japan, acting as accomplices for the tiger, are guilty of death, and everyone should eat their flesh.

Writing "My Feelings" 233

— Ke Ding'an

(1)

I often daydream like this, if the sea ban had not been lifted at that time, would our Chinese people still not have made progress by now? Also, if the sea ban had not been lifted at that time, our Chinese people would certainly still be living generation after generation. They would not die as soon as they were born. Looking at Chinese history, it is progressing generation after generation, and there is no fact of one generation regressing after another. In the past, China's prestige really shocked the world. Who knew that now, whether in diplomacy or commerce, there is nothing that is not restricted by foreigners, trampled by foreigners, and unable to break free. I think this problem comes from the opening of the sea ban. Since the opening of the sea ban, goods from various countries have come one after another, creating the Chinese people's habit of using foreign goods, which has become more and more serious until now. Even wearing a suit is not beautiful, living in a foreign house is not comfortable, eating big dishes is not satisfying, and traveling by car is not happy... (This is talking about the rich, and ordinary people certainly cannot do it; but a small amount of foreign goods promotion is inevitable.) If the sea ban had not been lifted, they would not abandon Chinese silk or cloth clothes, abandon Chinese-style gorgeous residences, move away from the delicacies of the mountains and seas, and stop riding in cars and palanquins.

"Humans are curious animals!" This is true. Because of their curiosity, they will always like the new and dislike the old. Only by liking the new and disliking the old can they abandon the essence of national goods and use the dross of foreign goods. I can't understand this reason at all.

"Is it good to open the sea ban, or is it good not to open it?"

(2)

In Shanghai, some people call foreign goods "goods from the road." What a good term "goods from the road"! How much praise it gets! The trendsetter, if he wears a foreign-made dress, he must like to boast in front of his friends, "This is a genuine 'goods from the road'!" His friends will definitely echo, "That's great, how much does each foot of this kind of 'goods from the road' cost?" Now the times have changed slightly. If you really wear a foreign-made dress, because the country is in trouble, you don't want to say, "This is 'goods from the road'," you want to say, "Look, how good are national goods!" I think: wearing foreign goods on the body and saying about wearing foreign goods in the mouth is an unforgivable sin. If you wear foreign goods and say you are wearing Chinese goods, I think the sin should be aggravated by one level. This is not only ruining national goods, but also related to your own personality.

There are also some women who do not understand the times. Of course, they do not know whether they are Western or Eastern goods. They only know that foreign goods are always fashionable and new. They make them to wear on their bodies and say to their companions, "This is 'goods from the road'." The women who say this sentence are probably parasites who are not responsible for making a living. Their consumption power is very considerable, but they all consume on foreigners and have to vigorously promote it to foreigners. This is really foolish. Those who have the responsibility of husbands can advise them!

(3)

I heard a friend who is familiar with the cotton cloth business say to me sincerely, "Now the general unscrupulous merchants are really confused and are selling Oriental goods there at a loss!" I heard it and seemed a little unbelievable. This is an ancient Chinese proverb: "Do thousands of things, do not do things at a loss." Could it be that they are selling Oriental goods there at a loss? This seems a little incomprehensible. After careful investigation, it turned out to be true. Because those unscrupulous merchants only seek their own interests and do not care about the interests of others. They put forward one or two kinds of inferior goods, mark them cheaply, and attract customers. In this way, the general blind public only knows that the goods are cheap, so how can they think that these are inferior goods! As for them, they use inferior goods to seduce buyers, which can also involve other goods and reap their benefits. The danger of their intentions is like snakes and scorpions! Although there are ×× groups that still resolutely warn, it is also of no avail. I think this "serving national goods" purpose should be embraced by oneself, that is reliable. If you want others to urge and warn you, the best result can only be effective now, not forever! Having said that, to serve national goods, relying solely on propaganda seems to be of no avail. The first thing is to transform people's hearts; transforming people's hearts is such a difficult thing!

Introduction to New Agricultural Tools

National Goods Rice Milling Machine 234

— Jing

The Danxin brand rice milling machine produced by Ding Yongyi Factory in Jinhui Bridge, Fengxian, can be said to be perfect and without any regrets. Ding Yongyi Factory was originally a rice sieve factory specializing in manufacturing rice machine sieves, and its business was very prosperous. The owner, Mr. Ding Shiru, likes to study mechanical science. Five years ago, he saw a rice milling machine produced in Japan somewhere. He studied it carefully, drew it into a picture, and hired workers to imitate it after returning. On the day the machine was completed, the test was good! The villagers competed to buy and use it. Over the past five years, it has been repeatedly improved and has become more perfect!

The structure of this machine is not very complicated, and the only raw materials required are wood and iron. Wood is used to make the machine body, which is naturally sourced from domestic production. That is, other accessories such as "iron nails," "iron teeth," and "iron wheels," except for "iron nails," which are purchased from domestic screws from hardware stores at sea, the rest are all manufactured by themselves through sand casting. Therefore, it can be called a purely domestic rice milling machine! In addition, as a result of years of improvement, the machine body has been slightly widened so that three or four people can work at the same time. The "iron teeth" on the machine shaft have also been increased compared to before, in order to increase its working efficiency. Even the wheel teeth at the junction of the large and small pulleys have been greatly changed to make it easier to rotate and increase the speed. Therefore, the work of three people and one machine can mill about ten acres of rice a day; compared with the previous rice mill, it is more than three times higher! With such a good domestic new agricultural tool! Isn't it worth introducing it?

Vase 236

— Yiyi Guan Zhu

Now in the 20th century, men and women pay attention to equality. Since men can serve in society, naturally, women must also work in the professional industry. This is undeniable.

However, we know that since the beginning of the world, men have not earned any nicknames or honorary titles for serving in society. However, female clerks sitting in the writing room are now called "vases" by men. Is this insulting them, or is it talking about equality?

Since they cannot get respect, naturally, they will be insulted and casually regarded as "vases" by men.

However, it is quite difficult to think of this honorary title for a while.

Short Story

Qiaoqi's Ball 237

— Qin Shouou

Qiaoqi was very happy in his heart when he went to school today, because yesterday his father had bought him a pink little ball, which could bounce three feet high with one pat, which was really a very fun thing.

"Huisheng, look, how good is this ball!" As soon as he entered the school gate, Qiaoqi couldn't wait to present his little ball to his friend Huisheng, who was also seven years old. But Huisheng looked at it and seemed not to pay any attention. Qiaoqi felt very puzzled. Later, Huisheng also held a ball.

"Look at mine, isn't it much bigger than yours?" Huisheng's ball was indeed several times larger than Qiaoqi's ball, and there were stripes on it, and the color was yellow. Many children looked at it and said that Huisheng's ball was good, and Qiaoqi's ball was not good.

Qiaoqi hid the ball in a fit of anger. When he went back for lunch, he was anxious to start negotiations with his father, and also told the style and color of Huisheng's ball, asking his father to buy the same one back.

"Ah! Child, that is an Oriental product! The hawkers on the road don't know the details, so they sell it there randomly, but we must not buy it: your ball is small, but it is always Chinese national goods, which is much better than their Oriental goods!" Father explained this way.

After listening, Qiaoqi still happily hugged his little ball to school. When he saw Huisheng, he smiled at him:

"What you bought is an Oriental product, are you embarrassed?" Huisheng certainly refused to admit that it was an Oriental product. The two children argued, and the classmates did not know who was right and who was wrong. Later, the teacher came and took a look at Huisheng's ball. It was indeed an Oriental product, so he told everyone. Huisheng couldn't help crying in embarrassment.

A day later, Huisheng also taught his father to buy a national goods little ball like Qiaoqi's, and the teacher praised him.

Spring and Autumn

Divine Will 238

— Yang Yusheng

Chinese people have always revered Heaven, so they place great importance on 'Divine Will.'

Now that 'human affairs' have deteriorated beyond repair, all expressions of sorrow, grief, and resentment seem largely unnecessary. Because everything about China, whether present or future, has long been predestined by Heaven, and cannot be salvaged by human effort. Helpless as we are, if our hearts are truly bursting with pain, we should shout 'Heaven' a few more times. 'People' are unreliable, especially since no one even pays attention to you! Since the September 18th Incident, China has constantly relied on the League of Nations. If the Western powers had sufficient strength, they might have come to the Far East and, disregarding appearances, spoken a word of justice. But they are too busy looking after themselves; how could they have time for your Chinese affairs? Therefore, Japan disregards everything and boldly advances into the Great Wall, North China, and even... Since China has no one to turn to for help, naturally it can only retreat helplessly. Is this not the will of Heaven?

The League of Nations cannot help China; if China could have used all its strength to resist Japan, perhaps it would not have deteriorated to this state. But instead, everything is chaotic and confusing. 'Internal pacification' is considered more urgent, so where is there spare strength to discuss 'external resistance'? Is this not the will of Heaven?

Although the Red bandits are bound to restrain 'external resistance,' if the Southwest authorities could take responsibility for 'internal pacification,' the Central government's three or four hundred thousand troops could certainly be used for 'external resistance.' But the Southwest remains in a state of wait-and-see, and has never sent troops. Is this not the will of Heaven?

These are just the major examples. Besides these, there are many minor signs, such as the floods and droughts of recent years, the rebellions in Xinjiang and Tibet, the internal strife in Shandong, Sichuan, and Guizhou, the wavering attitude of the southwestern provinces, and, down to the rampant activities of traitorous merchants, all happening together, without delay, during the most serious times of national crisis. The court and the people are bewildered and do not know what to do. Since the beginning of mankind, there has never been such chaos! Is this not the will of Heaven?

I have always been optimistic about the domestic situation. But seeing so many manifestations of the will of Heaven, I cannot help but utter a sigh of 'Alas.' This sigh contains the hidden pain of having to save, wanting to save but being unable to, watching death without being able to save, and having no way to save. But once I think of this as the will of Heaven, I have no choice but to give up!

Alas, the rise and fall, the survival and destruction of a nation, though attributed to human affairs, are not, in truth, ordained by Heaven!

Tears 239

— Zheng Chuyou

Women are the most prone to tears; using summer rain as a symbol of women's tears is quite appropriate.

In summer, as long as the weather is somewhat hot and stuffy, or after a few strong gusts of wind, these subtle little reasons can cause it to rain in the summer; although it doesn't last long, what's called a 'passing shower' that stops in a few minutes, the rain falls as fiercely as a waterfall, and the raindrops are as thick as bamboo sticks, which can be a little frightening when encountered. Women's tears are like summer rain; as long as their hearts are a little unhappy, they experience some external stimuli, or their bodies have a minor ailment, their tears will flow wildly like summer rain. To vent the sorrow hidden in their hearts and the pain in their bodies, these wildly flowing tears are the only method for women!

As for the tears of us men, they are like winter rain, reluctant to fall easily. Although sometimes a few heroic tears may be shed, it's not that men don't have inner sorrow or physical pain; it's just that men are more able to endure than women, more able to put things behind them. Even if it is really unbearable for a moment, and they can't put it behind them, often, at the height of grief, they cannot even shed tears because most of their tears have already turned into blood and strength, and the few remaining tears are swallowed instead of flowing outward!

The Nation of Words 240

— Xu Benxi

Our China is the great nation of words; this cannot be denied.

When young people fall in love, when men and women become friends, they always start by saying to each other: let's form an alliance of scholarly pursuits. In fact, if the spirit of love were entrusted to words, then, even if it's not nauseating, I think we could achieve mutual understanding on various thoughts, which wouldn't be bad. But reality is reality, and after the mask of love is removed, they will go step by step to do some things that young people do, and the result is that the woman hires a lawyer to accuse the man of 'seduction,' 'breach of contract,' and what is called 'starting with intimacy and ending with abandonment.' The lawyer's indictment is written with ten thousand flowery words, and the newspaper's account is written with flowery language, making people feel nauseated and infatuated. If we carefully try to understand, then we can discover that this game of love is fundamentally dominated by words, beginning with an exchange of words and ending with a resolution in words.

When warlords want a civil war, they must first issue a grand and extensive telegram. When the government wants non-resistance, it also declares how long it will resist. In essence, it's just officialdom in writing.

Only we comrades who engage in textual labor are often harmed by careless writing. If a word is used in a frightening way, it is the XX party. Looking at the several literary inquisitions of the early Qing Dynasty, one can know that scholars cannot misuse words, and this is even more intense today.

In short, words also have a hierarchy. The superiors can say whatever they want to the inferiors, but the inferiors must be cautious when speaking to the superiors.

The Skill of Words 241

— Fen Hua

The Sichuan warlords have launched another war, and the Anti-Civil War League of this city

has telegraphed both sides, requesting them to prioritize the national crisis and cease fighting against external enemies.

They were quite receptive, and Deng Xihou sent a reply. The wording of the reply was really good, using the ability of literary skill to the fullest.

He said: 'I have always admired your esteemed association's concern for the national crisis and efforts to stop internal strife. I, Xihou, have always loved peace and been ashamed of internal wars. Now, the more I retreat, the more Liu Wenhui advances, making it extremely difficult for the entire army to retreat. At this time of national crisis, he disregards everything! You, esteemed gentlemen, are the lucky stars of peace, calling out in all directions. I urge you to quickly propose effective sanctions against those who provoke war without cause, to uphold justice.' It turns out that he greatly admires the esteemed association which is concerned with the national crisis, and he greatly loves peace, and is ashamed of internal wars, but because the other side is advancing, the whole army is extremely angry and difficult to restrain, so he is not responsible. Not only is he not responsible, but he is also placing the responsibility on the esteemed gentlemen of the association, demanding effective sanctions to uphold justice. If the esteemed association does not have effective sanctions, then it has nothing to do with him, and it is the fault of the esteemed association for not fulfilling its duty, and the esteemed association should no longer ask him to cease fighting. It's really wonderful, and we'll have to see how Liu Wenhui replies. I imagine that Liu also understands the skill of words, and perhaps Liu's wording is even better than Deng's, because this is already a masterpiece of the Sichuan warlords. In short, one way or another, they won't be wrong, and the mistake really lies in the fact that China has that blessed land, the land of Sichuan, where they can close the door and put on a show!

Modernity Knows No National Crisis 242

— Gu Wohfo

'National crisis' is certainly not something personal, or belonging to a few people. All the people of China, and everything Chinese, are being suppressed by this impending national crisis. 'Saving the nation' is a cry that has been squeezed out by this impending national crisis! But there are exceptions to everything. 'Modernity' in China knows no national crisis. National crisis will not befall 'modernity.' Modernity knows no national crisis, so there is fundamentally no need to save the nation.

The modern dance halls, the modern cinemas, the modern cafes, and the companies that sell modernity, the agencies that promote modernity, and the places that flaunt modernity. Whether you have the eyes of a thousand miles or the ears of the wind, you won't find any trace of national crisis in this area. Even the omnipresent and ever-penetrating national crisis, upon reaching these modern locales, can only sigh in despair and retreat in hesitation. Moreover, there is an ironclad piece of evidence:

The special correspondent of Shen Bao, Geng Ya, said in 'Notes from the War Zone': ': Returning to the adjutant's office, I saw the orderly packing his luggage. Surprised, I asked him why. I learned that the military headquarters was about to move to a certain place. The reporter hurriedly left the city. The moonlight was desolate, and I felt gloomy! At that time, there were petite and exquisite modern women walking together along the sandy road, accompanied by soldiers carrying suitcases and luggage. I guessed that they were the dependents of officials, but I dared not be sure.' Isn't this account a good illustration of 'modernity knows no national crisis'? Let's not worry about whether she is the official's dependent. But modernity is still modernity. So, even though the impending national crisis is progressing rapidly, how can it catch up with the particularly fast running of modernity's two fleshy legs? Tell me, is there any hope for the national crisis to catch up with modernity? As for those who are not modern? Because they are not modern, they can only let the national crisis strike head-on, let the national crisis encircle us heavily, what else can they say?

Scientific Anecdotes

Various Things About Biology 244

— Xinong

We all have this experience, right? Women are particularly skilled at casual conversation. As long as they find a match (they'll find one very easily, and those matches are, of course, mostly women), they'll go on and on and on, talking and talking, starting with the cat of the family to the east and going all the way to the dog of the family to the west. Even if they talk for two or three hours straight, they don't get tired at all. Moreover, it seems this is the case in both ancient times and in foreign countries. It's not just women in our China who are like this. Why do women like to talk so much? According to research by two German physiologists, women's vocal cords are lighter than men's, so they vibrate more easily and produce sound waves. That's an interesting discovery.

We all know the functions of the skin: it protects muscles and organs, and it also carries out respiration and excretion. But according to recent research, it also contains a bactericidal substance. So, in addition to the above-mentioned effects, it also has the direct function of preventing infectious diseases from entering. According to experiments, if we put bacteria such as typhoid bacteria on the skin, it will destroy 90% to 95% of all the bacteria in an instant. However, this function is directly proportional to the cleanliness of the skin. If it is too dirty, it will completely lose its effect.

We can usually observe that the feathers of birds and animals, even without being lubricated with any grease or water, are neat and smooth. Unlike human hair, it takes time, money, and patience to obtain temporary neatness and beauty after a procedure. They are both hair, why are humans given so little of it? According to recent research by the German scientist Exner, there is also the effect of electricity in between. For example, in birds, the feathers are arranged very densely. Because of their mutual friction, electricity is generated. Fine feathers are the cathode, and feathers are the anode. Although there is no distinction between fine and coarse hair in animals, there is also a difference in thickness. Coarse hair is like bird feathers, bearing positive electricity, and fine hair bears negative electricity. According to the principle of opposites attracting each other, they appear neat and smooth. But at the same time, because of the repulsion of opposite charges between the fine hairs, the fine hairs are evenly spread over the body. Therefore, this electrical effect has two meanings for birds and animals. One is that the fluffiness of the fine hair prevents body heat from dissipating, and the other is that the smoothness of the feathers makes it difficult for rainwater and other harmful substances to enter. Human hair is completely one color, with no distinction between thick and thin, so the result of friction can only produce electrodes of the same charge, which repel each other. This is also why hair is not easy to comb straight when it is dry. When it is wetted with water, and the electricity is conducted away, it is easy to comb neatly. The growth of children is generally thought by people to be directly proportional to time and nutrition. But according to recent research published by Professor Lang Kai of Harvard University, the facts are surprisingly different. The growth of children is not only related to good nutrition but is also greatly influenced by the seasons. Lang has made two measurements of body length and weight on healthy children in nurseries, and the results show that the increase in weight can be divided into three periods according to its speed of increase: for two-year-old children, the fastest is between September and December, the slowest is between May and August, and January to April is relatively average. The larger children (from three to six years old) grow fastest between June and November, followed by May, and slowest between December and April. At the same time, the increase in body length can be divided into four periods, the fastest from April to July, followed by September to November, followed by August, and slowest from December to March. Moreover, whether large or small children, the results are exactly the same, not only divided into four periods, but the order of fast and slow is also the same.

The abominableness and harm of mosquitoes can be said to be known to everyone, so there is no need to say more. But the effective methods to drive them away that humans know so far are very few. Dr. Gelefu of Germany, in order to find a more effective defense method, has done many experiments in the tropics. He made seventeen boxes of different colors, placed mosquito-attracting items inside, and placed them where mosquitoes gathered. As a result, most of the mosquitoes gathered in the dark blue boxes. Scarlet, dark gray, and dark colors had very few. White, purple, green, and other colors had even fewer. And there were no mosquitoes at all in the yellow boxes. The experiments were all the same. From this we know that mosquitoes do not like the color yellow, or they do not have a yellow sense. We can use this to protect against mosquitoes, such as changing window curtains, tents, and lights to yellow for a try.

Free Talk

Nonsense 270

— Qifan

To adapt to the needs of the times, I once wanted to organize a "Nonsense Company" to serve all aspects of society. It is a pity that it did not succeed, otherwise it could have helped and shown off in the grand movements of saving the country through dancing, saving the country through opera, saving the country through entertainment, saving the country through religious services, and even saving the country through exhibitions. It is not that I say that these things are entirely nonsense, I want to advocate that nonsense can also be a start to saving the country.

This clearly does not refer to the national salvation tone of Dr. Hu Shih, nor is it the movie stars Hu Die, Hu Shan, Hu Jia Ping, etc., nor the tones of musical instruments such as the huqin and the drum. Nonsense is just nonsense in Shanghai dialect. The characteristic of nonsense lies in its inexplicable, dazed and confused, but the surface is very enthusiastic, very decent, and extremely serious. The most wonderful thing is that the people who do it know that it is impossible to do, they know that it has no effect, but they still bite the bullet and do it, with an unattainable spirit. At the beginning, there was indeed the fearless spirit of the Buddha saying that if I don’t go to hell, who will, but the result is a mess, and you can’t blame him.

From ancient times, judging the good and evil of deeds depends on the motive. It is the behavior of snobbish villains to judge heroes by success or failure. The result of nonsense is naturally that there are few successes and many failures, but this does not prevent it from being a good deed. Moreover, there are many ways to save the country. If everyone insists that what they are advocating is the only way to save the country, it will inevitably lead to internal strife before the country is saved, which is extremely shameful, so nonsense is indispensable. Nonsense means harmony everywhere, and agreement everywhere. Saying what others say and echoing what others say is the characteristic of nonsense. Following in footsteps like a shadow is also a characteristic of nonsense. Moreover, there are also those who surpass the scope of echoing and imitating and bravely advance forward. They can march and send troops without goals or plans, and execute affairs without preconceived ideas. That spirit of courage is really beyond the reach of ordinary people.

Courage is courage, but it is not enthusiastic. If this road does not work, you can take another one, which is also walking casually, without any choice. There is no attachment at all, and the ability to be extremely round and smooth, because there is no overall predetermined plan, so it doesn’t matter how you change it, and that’s where the ease of living of nonsense lies. They are always optimistic, and there are solutions to everything, but the result is that nothing goes wrong. Nonsense is the brotherhood of confusion.

Nonsense will never have a clear attitude, and it is not allowed to have it, because it is inherently vague and obscure. Things seem to be in progress and seem to be stagnant, the attitude seems to be affirmative and seems to be negative. Unless it is beyond saving, nonsense will never fail, and by that time, even if it is not nonsense, it will fail. Speaking of it, it is a kind of aging and twilight. The Chinese nation is on the verge of aging, and there is a lot of nonsense everywhere. From now on, governing and saving the country cannot be a major plan without nonsense. Alas!

Dongting and West Lake 271

— Xing Zhi

I grew up by Dongting Lake; however, from a young age, I was

in awe of West Lake's great reputation. Every time I read the line, "To compare West Lake to Xi Shi, whether lightly or heavily adorned, both are fitting," a vision of an unparalleled beauty stirred in my young heart, reflecting a bright and beautiful West Lake.

I've been away from my hometown for six or seven years. The vast expanse of eight hundred *li*,

where the lake and sky blend into one at Dongting, truly makes me yearn in my dreams. However, last autumn, I went to visit the West Lake, which I had long admired. I nestled in the embrace of Xi Shi, and although it was only for three short days, I saw the West Lake in its sunny splendor, its somber mood, and after the rain. I truly thank Heaven for such thorough arrangements for me.

West Lake is indeed exceptionally beautiful, a

quintessential image of Eastern beauty. In its sunny disposition, it is so bright and lovely; in its somber mood, it is so dignified; and after the rain, it is like a freshly bathed beauty, lightly veiled in silk, further enhancing its allure. After touring West Lake, I couldn't help but exclaim, "My hometown has no such beautiful lakes and mountains!"

However, to say, "My hometown has no such beautiful lakes and mountains," is, after all,

an affront to Dongting. Who can say Dongting Lake is not beautiful? However, Dongting's beauty is of a different kind. If we say West Lake is a beauty, then Dongting can be described as a hero. Because Dongting is magnificent, not exquisite; it is grand, not bright. There are no willows dancing in the spring breeze, nor warbling orioles, only colossal waves crashing against the sky, roaring out ancient songs of injustice. The raging torrents rush eastward, sweeping away figures from throughout history. There are no young men and women gently rowing in small boats, whispering sweet nothings, only giant warships racing by, black smoke rising into the air, and deep within the reeds, numerous heroic figures of the rivers and lakes, commanding wind and thunder. Facing the boundless lake where the sky and water meet, and the ever-changing scenery shrouded in mist, one can only stand upright and gaze from afar, solemnly concentrating. The sky is always so vast, the lake always so wide, that even if you want to praise it, you cannot find a suitable eulogy. Fan Zhongyan, in his *Yueyang Tower Record*, described Dongting as: "Surrounded by distant mountains, swallowing long rivers, vast and boundless, with no end in sight; sunrise glow and evening shadows, myriad phenomena." I think this is still insufficient to describe the grandeur and magnificence of Dongting.

West Lake, after all, is exquisite. Precisely because it is exquisite,

people can play with it. All around the lake roads, cars roll by. Beneath Baochu Pagoda, red buildings are hidden. All the dignitaries and wealthy, the vulgar city monks, all with the intention of buying a smile with a thousand gold coins, squeeze into West Lake's embrace. Boats in the lake are as numerous as carp. Red men and green women, strings and songs. When the breeze rises, the lake water also ripples with a golden smile. It has already put on a capitalist coat and has become a courtesan. It no longer has that natural and simple beauty. Compared to Dongting, which can only be viewed from afar and not be profaned, West Lake should feel sorry for itself and pale in comparison.

In Dongting Lake, there is Jun Mountain, a verdant

dot, just like a blue snail in a crystal plate. On the mountain are the Langyin Pavilion and the Tingtao Pavilion. There are the tombs of Emperors Ehuang and Nuying, the well from which Liu Yi once descended into the sea to deliver a letter for the Dragon Princess, and bamboo stalks marked with tear stains. Yueyang Tower stands majestically across the bank, facing it solemnly. Fishermen's songs rise and fall by the lakeside, and the sound of oars echoes gently. It is truly a natural painting, beautiful, good, and true.

It has been seven years since I left Dongting Lake. I ask, have the

sand and dust of my hometown covered the footprints of my youthful wanderings? Raising my head and looking west, I often feel deeply lost. A message to the lake and mountains: if the lake and mountains remain unchanged in the future, I shall return. Written in Shanghai on May 24th.

Little Local Tyrant 272

— Bing Xin

This was an unexpectedly pleasant surprise. When Shurong led me into a refined and clean small Western-style building, I truly

couldn't believe that such a house could be found in Longyan.

"Hey, how can there be such a nice house in Longyan?"

"We must thank the owner of this house, that local tyrant gentry!" she replied with a smiling face and a slightly comical tone.

"Ah, so it belongs to a local tyrant gentry! No wonder it's so

beautiful."

Although I said it was beautiful, compared to the Western-style houses in Shanghai, this could only be considered a dilapidated toilet. Although the house had two stories and its architectural style was somewhat Westernized, it had been damaged by the army, and the doors, window railings, etc. were all gone. The walls were covered with various slogans. Shurong had only made two doors after she arrived, but there were still no windows, and the large holes were only covered with two large sheets of paper.

"How can this have any ventilation?" When Shu brought me to

the room she had prepared for me, I cried out as soon as I entered the door. It turned out that the beautiful house was just an embroidered pillow.

"Hey, you still complain about the lack of ventilation. You won't find a second

house as good as this in Longyan. Don't underestimate it. You'd be scared to death if you saw the houses the common people live in, which truly have no ventilation and no light."

...After listening to Shu's words, I could only stick out my tongue. I couldn't help but feel dissatisfied and hurriedly piled the bedding on the bed frame. When I saw the drawerless table, supported by only a broken board and four legs, I was disappointed again.

"Do you know how much effort it took to borrow this table from

their office?" Shu seemed to have seen what I was thinking, so she explained it to me very carefully. I was naturally very grateful to her. A room with bare walls like this... Shi's family... exclusively he... borrowed two stools for me, otherwise, I would have to stand at attention as soon as I entered the door.

The first time I saw the woman whose two eyes were fixedly

staring at me, she greeted Shu with a smile. Shu told her that I had just come from Zhangzhou today.

"Who is this woman?" I was a little surprised at how familiar Shu seemed

with her.

"She's the owner of the house, the wife of the local tyrant

gentry."

"Where's her husband?"

"He ran away to Xiamen and hasn't come back yet."

"Does she still have any property?"

"No, all her fields have been taken to be distributed to the

peasants. She has nothing else. She's really pitiful now. Her ten-year-old daughter picks coal every day, and her two sons are too young and can only eat. Therefore, her life has been getting poorer and poorer lately."

"This is the result the local tyrant gentry deserves."

"Look, this is her youngest son. Look

at how fierce and stupid he looks. His two big eyes are like a tiger's eyes, with that kind of foolish and dull expression, as annoying as a pig."

Observing the little local tyrant standing next to me, his two eyes were indeed particularly large, almost like bull's eyes, but the light shining from them was dull, stagnant, foolish, and annoying. Xiao Hang told me that no matter what you asked him, he would always stand at attention and answer, and with particular vigor. For example, if you asked him, "Have you eaten yet?" "Yes!"

"Don't stand here!" "Yes!" His tone and attitude were exactly like a soldier treating his superior officer, truly amusing. (To be continued)

Editorial Office 273

In this day and age, it is difficult to speak, and even more difficult to wield a pen. This

isn't to say: "Fortune and misfortune have no doors, it is only men who invite them." It really is "The world has this," and "common people" should "not discuss." The editor respectfully offers a heartfelt plea to all the literary giants in the country: from now on, talk more about romance and less about complaints, so that both the author and the editor can have a rest. If you must discuss lengths and shortcomings, and recklessly talk about important matters, then to stuff it into the wastebasket is something we cannot bear to do, and to publish it on the news is something we cannot do, trapping the editor in a dilemma, which is inevitably lacking in empathy. As the saying goes, "Those who understand the times are outstanding," and the editor dares to say this to all the literary giants in the country. This humble plight, please understand and consider. The Editor

Carrot Top 274

— Written by JULES KENARA, translated by Lin Qu

Red Cheeks Two (Continued)

Carrot Top peeped for a long time again. He was afraid that Weiaolong would suddenly run back, but Masuo had already curled up into a ball and covered his head with the quilt, but he was not asleep. He was recalling the inexplicable event that had just occurred. He did not see anything in this matter that could make him suffer. In the dark quilt, the image of Weiaolong clearly floated before his eyes, and this image was as gentle as the images of those women who often excited him in his dreams.

Carrot Top was too lazy to wait any longer. His eyelids closed as if feeling magnetic force. He forced himself to open his eyes and look at the very small gas lamp: but after three small bubbles appeared from the lamp nozzle, making soft sounds, he fell asleep.

Three

The next morning, when everyone washed their faces with basins, dipped the corner of a towel in a little cold water, and gently wiped their cold cheekbones, Carrot Top glared fiercely at Masuo, and tried his best to look savage. He gritted his teeth and scolded him in a shrill voice:

"Rabbit! Rabbit!"

Masuo's cheeks flushed red, but he still answered him gently, and almost with a pleading look:

"Since I told you that nothing happened, what are you making a fuss about!"

The school supervisor came to check if their hands were clean. The students stood in two rows, mechanically stretched out their hands, first the backs of their hands, and then quickly turned their hands over, and immediately retracted them to a warm place - inserted in their pockets, or stuffed into the lukewarm down quilt of a nearby bed. Usually, Weiaolong did not look carefully, but today, unfortunately, he found that Carrot Top's hands were not clean. Ordered to go to the faucet to wash again, Carrot Top felt dissatisfied. In fact, there were some blue stains on his hands, but Carrot Top stubbornly said that this was the precursor to frostbite. Someone must have a personal grudge against him.

Weiaolong had to send him to the headmaster's office.

The headmaster, who had gotten up early, was preparing a history lesson in his office, which was wallpapered with a dim green color, to teach to the older students when he had free time. He forcefully tapped his fat fingers on the table, distinguishing various major stages: here was the decline of the Roman Empire; in the middle was the Turkish invasion of Constantinople; a little further was the endless modern history that no one knew when it began.

He was wearing a large nightgown, and several silk ribbons held up his firm chest, like ropes tied to stone pillars. Obviously, this gentleman ate too much; the lines on his face were coarse and slightly shiny. He spoke in a loud voice, the same as when he spoke to the ladies; the wrinkles on his neck undulated slowly and rhythmically on his stiff collar. Also, his round eyes and thick mustache were very noticeable.

Carrot Top stood in front of him, taking off his hat and placing it between his legs, so as to maintain freedom of movement.

The headmaster asked in a terrible voice:

"What's the matter?"

"Sir, the school supervisor said my hands were not clean and sent me here, but this is a false accusation!"

Carrot Top confidently stretched out his hands again, first the backs of his hands, and then turned them over. He turned his hands back and forth, proving that the school supervisor had wronged him.

"Ah! Wronged you!" the headmaster said, "Four days of holiday ban, my child!"

Talks

Adam and Eve 275

— Niu

The Adam and Eve of the Bible are as absurd and groundless as Pangu in Chinese history. Whether

they existed as people or events is still a question. Unexpectedly, a Reuters dispatch yesterday from Turkey said that the Turkish people have now made a new discovery that Adam and Eve were indeed produced in that region. Because of various textual researches on the word "family" and "era," Adam and Eve are determined to be Turkish people, just like someone with the surname Zhou insists on recognizing King Wen as their ancestor, and someone with the surname Jiang insists on recognizing Taigong as their family origin. It is equally laughable. But I dare not say whether Adam and Eve admit this. I can only put this matter aside and ask Adam and Eve before talking about it again.

A Reuters dispatch from Harbin on the 21st said that the nudist society in this area recently formed a club, named it "Adam and Eve," and held its first meeting in Krestovsky, and on the island

they sunbathed naked for three hours, etc.

I highly approve. Adam and Eve were originally men and women who did not wear pants, and were the ancestors of the primitive era. Since sunbathing was invented abroad, it has become quite popular in various places. Last year, Hong Kong also had such an organization, with both Chinese and foreign men and women. However, foreign women were still shy, and although they joined, they did not actually practice it. Only the Chinese women who joined were very enthusiastic. From this point of view, foreign women are not thoroughly civilized, and Chinese women are thoroughly civilized. Taking the Chinese women of recent years as an example, marriage is absolutely free, the fashion is constantly changing, and the three thousand worries of hair are also cut clean. Such innovative styles are all well-organized. From these many behaviors, one can see the degree of civilization of Chinese women.

However, it is not clear from the dispatch whether there are Chinese women participating in the current "Harbin Adam and Eve Society," so I dare not speculate. But based on the facts, I am afraid that Chinese women are not without participation. Soviet Russia is originally a communist country, not only communist, but also has communal wives. The marriage system has long been completely overthrown. However, under certain circumstances, as long as the other party agrees, they can be husband and wife for a short period of time. Therefore, nakedness or non-nakedness is originally not a problem. But China still has some constraints of the marriage system in freedom, and there is still some unfreedom. Therefore, Chinese people like sunbathing, and Russians naturally agree. Even I personally would never oppose it, for two reasons:

(1) Cultural progress is originally a reductionist style. Life in the past was more comfortable every day, but life now is more difficult every day. Culture in the past progressed step by step, but culture now regresses step by step. That is, everything else is like this. These are all reductionist performances. Therefore, Mencius said, "The difference between humans and animals is slight." The scholars of the rationalist school noted, "Slight means that it can be known that there is originally no great difference between humans and animals." Going a step further, humans are only one of the animals, then why can't animals be naked?

(2) Didn't the Premier say that the greatest elements of life are clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and that clothing is the first of the four major elements? Of course, the problem of clothing and food is the most difficult to solve. If everyone did not wear clothes, wouldn't they save a lot of trouble and countless economies? The *huaer sha* of summer and the brocade *zhou* of winter, etc., would not be needed. The first element of the four major elements would not be difficult. Wouldn't it be interesting if the world were full of men and women who did not wear pants?

Based on the above two reasons, I extremely approve of "Adam and Eveism." Originally, it is most fashionable now to go barefoot and not wear socks. If you don't even wear pants, wouldn't it be even more fashionable? Amen.

Arts and Literature

On Hearing That the Japanese Army is Invading Southward and Tianjin and Beijing are in Imminent Danger, I Compose This Poem with Tears 276

— Ding Chong

Looking north at the dangerous city before the setting sun, the *xiao xiao* barbarian horses

cross You and Yan. The righteous army is as empty and fierce as Suiyang's,

the grand strategy still seeks the completeness of Zhongsu. Sleeping on firewood, the Yue people

will eventually avenge their shame, the stalks burn in the Wei household, how can that be wise?

I am ashamed that I do not have a sky-supporting hand, and only imitate Jia Sheng

weeping with tears.

How will the court officials make their decisions? I see the Jin soldiers

crossing the river again. Rejecting difficulties, Lu Lian ultimately fails,

allowing Qin Hui to seek peace by stealth. Turning my head to look at the Great Wall, who is in charge now?

My heart is pricked by the continual encroachment on our national territory.

After all, good charcoal comes from curved chimneys, I rely

on regret for a long time.

An Ordinary Tragedy 277

— Huai Zhuang

An unfortunate event finally befell Min'er. Her

loving father and mother both abandoned this adorable little bird, intending to ascend to heaven alone. Thus, the responsibility of raising her naturally falls to her uncle.

"Min'er," on the fourth day Min'er was at her uncle's house, her aunt urged her, "You are already

fifteen years old, and still just love to play. Haven't you seen the daughter of Wang's mother next door? She, at thirteen years old, gets up early to wipe the tables, clean the windows, make the bed, and sweep the floor. There is nothing she can't do. During the day when she has free time, she also takes the frame and learns to embroider!"

"Unlike you..." Her aunt pointed at her,

continuing to speak, her tone seeming to become heavier, and from her face it could be seen that she had a disdainful expression. "Humph! Aren't you just a world apart from her?"

Also, the old woman across the street also said that today's women

are truly a joke. All day long, they don't know what they are doing. They have only learned many skills of flirting! Alas! Heaven knows! When they go to their husband's house in the future, I really don't know how much suffering they will have to endure!

"Min'er, if you don't listen to me now, in the future,

if no one comes to marry you, then don't blame me." Her aunt's tone was relatively soft. Then, she pointed to the coal briquette stove leaning against the wall in the kitchen and said, "Be good. Quickly light this coal briquette stove. Later, when your elder sister (her own daughter) gets up, she can go to school earlier!"

After half an hour of trying, Min'er finally failed.

Black coal dust stained her hands and face. At the same time, her tears also fell because of the coal gas. But her aunt still scolded her "stupid bug" over and over again.

At eight-thirty, Qianjie finally woke up from her pink dream. Because the coal stove was lit slowly today, the soup hadn't been stewed yet, so she just sat on the edge of the bed and got angry.

"Qian'er," Min'er's aunt said, "My good girl, don't

be angry. It's all Min'er's fault. Later, I will scold her severely." Pausing, she said as she bent down to button the unbuttoned clothes for her daughter, speaking softly and gently, "Your Indian silk *qipao* can be finished before lunch. This afternoon you can go to the movies with Yuanyuan across the street. Also, your rouge is used up, so you can buy some on the way."

"Get up quickly! Don't be angry!"

Qianjie's anger subsided a bit. She simply lay down on the

bed and acted spoiled, saying, "Then, where are my high-heeled leather shoes?"

"Those high-heeled leather shoes? Don't worry! I already

asked your father to buy them."

At this time, Qianjie's laughter and Min'er's sobs

had inadvertently become the symphony of life.

The water on the coal stove boiled, only making sounds in the pot,

as if decorating this ordinary tragedy.

Comfort.
