Shop Assistant Correspondence

I Want to Redeem Myself

Dear Editor,

I am not a shop assistant, nor an apprentice; I am a seventeen-year-old weak woman, wandering in a foreign land, without any relatives to rely on. Can you make an exception and reply to all my questions? Sir, I hope you will not despise me because of this, and help me find a bright future.

In the year I was born, my mother passed away; my father then married a stepmother. Unfortunately, when I was three years old, my father also passed away. The cruel stepmother sold me into a family when I was five years old to be a maid. At first, they treated me well and even sent me to school. Now, they treat me badly; if they are unhappy, they treat me as a "venting tool," beating and scolding me; they no longer let me study. I really cannot bear this ill-treatment and have long wanted to escape this prison. Currently, I have a friend who is willing to help me and even allow me to continue my studies. Therefore, I want to redeem myself. When they bought me, they spent seventy-five yuan, studying at a certain school cost sixty yuan, and studying at another school cost thirty yuan. I think I should give them one hundred and sixty-five yuan. Is this legally permissible? What should I do if they refuse?

Sir, please answer me. I am here, eagerly awaiting your response! Please do not disappoint me! Sincerely wish you good health.

Respectfully, Li Cuiying

X X X X

Editor's Note: Trafficking in persons is prohibited; indentures of servitude cannot be presented to the authorities. If you want to regain your freedom, you only need to hire a lawyer to write a letter to your master, expressing your intention, and at the same time, file a statement on your behalf. Now that you acknowledge that they treated you fairly well in the past and even allowed you to study, you are willing to give them one hundred and sixty-five yuan, which is already considered benevolent and just. In theory, they should agree immediately. If, by any chance, they refuse, you can seek legal assistance; with one hundred and sixty-five yuan, all the procedures can probably be handled properly.

However, you are only seventeen years old this year, and your experience is not yet deep enough. What is the relationship between that friend of yours and you? Is he a good person? Why is he willing to help you? Does he have an ulterior motive? Is his motive legitimate? You need to consider all these things carefully. If you are deceived by a wicked person for a moment and act rashly, or even cohabit with him, then your suffering will be endless! According to your letter, your current master cannot be considered extremely cruel, and the relationship of servitude can be terminated at any time. Cohabiting with a wicked person is like "trying to catch dry ashes in a leaky hand," and we cannot foresee what will happen to you! This is our concern; may the ladies carefully consider this themselves.

Notice for This Column 280

The purpose of setting up this column is to assist workers, shop assistants, apprentices, etc., in solving difficult problems. Those who write in should be satisfied with receiving a reply. In the past two months, thanks to the support of all circles, there have been more than ten inquiries every day. Although we hold the aspiration of answering every letter, we are limited by the facts. Except for the common problems that we consider to be shared by most people, which are published daily in the newspaper, the remaining problems that are unique to individuals are answered directly by this column in a letter. However, in recent days, we have received many letters that have not disclosed the address as required. We assume that the intention is to have them published in the newspaper, but a closer look at the content of the problems reveals that they are not very relevant to the general public. If we publish them one by one, not only will readers inevitably lose interest, but there is also no space to accommodate the thirteen or fourteen letters that arrive every day. We hope that future letters must be handled in accordance with the regulations of this column, especially the address must be disclosed, otherwise we will not reply. Please understand.

Shop Assistant Correspondence Column Regulations

(1) Purpose of Communication: This column aims to gather ideas, explain difficult problems, learn from each other, and enhance the happiness of life.

(2) Target Audience: The target audience of this column is limited to shop assistants, apprentices, and workers in terms of people, and only this city in terms of location.

(3) Content of Communication: Everything related to personal daily life, such as:

Novel

The Life of the Five Beauties (17) (Continued) 281

— Ling He

Fifteen: Competition

The next morning, very early, Miss Liu kissed Wenbin's forehead with sleepy eyes, stroking his blushing cheeks with infinite tenderness, revealing a bit of lingering affection. But the one sleeping in her arms was still sound asleep, from which it could be known that this night was indeed filled with indescribable deep love. Afterwards, Miss Liu suddenly realized that he should no longer be sleeping soundly on her bed, so she decided to wake him up. When he woke up and hugged her tightly again, she said:

"Poor child, you can go now."

"What? You're telling me to leave?"

"Yes, child. Because now is the time when you must leave here. Of course, I fully understand that I need your warmth, your embrace, but you also have to know that I can't fully commit myself to you yet. In fact, I have to serve other men who are more important than you. Darling, do you understand? I am sincerely loving you."

Of course, Zhang Wenbin could not help but be very unhappy, but unable to resist her gentle persuasion, he still lazily walked out of her room. But he always had to come back and ask her:

"Then who are you planning to receive now?"

"Why do you need to ask about this?" she said with a smile: "Darling, I'm telling you, you don't need to worry about my affairs. Now, go back and sleep well, quietly waiting for my orders. As long as it's convenient, maybe we can meet again tomorrow night. In short, please believe me, I have never loved any other man the way I love you. I feel that this is your greatest victory."

After he left, Manager Gu called once, saying that he couldn't come in the morning due to some business, and promised to see her again in the evening. On this day, Miss Liu was immersed in sweet memories. Perhaps this was the beginning of her luck. But in any case, she had now gained a new kind of stimulation, although this love made her excessively uneasy, as if her soul was bewitched by this newcomer.

Until the lights in the house were turned on again in the evening, and bank manager Mr. Gu was diligently pouring champagne for her, she was re-recognizing her life; she was still selling her life cheaply. However, Manager Gu was now indulging himself to the fullest; this was very clear to her.

After that, there was a burst of car horns outside, and Wu Gui was heard shouting in another room:

"Who's going to open the door? Another guest is here!"

Then He Xiang walked closer to Miss Liu and whispered a few words. Then she looked at Manager Gu and said with a smile:

"What's wrong with that? You bring her up here. Anyway, everyone knows each other."

"Who? Who's coming?" Manager Gu asked:

"She'll be here soon. You wait and see."

After a while, Minister Su walked in wearing brand new clothes. The manager immediately stood up and shouted loudly:

"Oh, it's you! Great! Great! Please sit down, please sit down. Hey, tell them to bring another glass!"

"Really, I didn't expect that we would meet here," Minister Su said as he sat down, stealing a glance at Miss Liu and then very politely greeting Manager Gu: "It's really great that we can talk here. Mr. Gu often comes here to visit?"

"No, today is the first time I've met Miss Yang."

"Oh? Me too; I only met her the day before yesterday."

"Then you have one more day of friendship than I do."

They were both very smart, and both believed that they were good at rhetoric. Only Miss Liu laughed loudly and immediately raised her glass and took a sip. Unfortunately, it caused a strong cough. Probably because the wine flowed into her trachea, this strong cough could not be stopped for a while. Until she ran into the bedroom and saw bloodstains in the sputum container, she could not help but wipe away her tears and sigh deeply. However, at this time, the two Chinese giants outside, she believed, must be having a very投機conversation.

Film Special

"Piano Heart Ripple" Performed at the Grand Theater 282

— Zhi Xiang

The long-publicized pantomime "Piano Heart Ripple" premiered at the Grand Theater on the 21st. The play can be regarded as the first collaboration between Chinese drama and symphony music. Judging from the performance results, it can be said to be a success.

The evening's program was divided into three sections. The first section was Chinese ancient music. First, the Datong Orchestra played Eastern music; the society has long been famous in society, and this time, participating in the grand event, both sides felt that they added luster to each other. The second was Wei Jun's pipa solo. This gentleman's technique is skilled, and the song "Huaiyin Pingchu" is even more sonorous, winning a lot of applause from the audience.

The second section was the symphonic works of the composer Afu Xia Lomufu. First, Mrs. Liu Jingfang sang Afu's "Qingwen's Death Song." The lyrics were compiled by Mr. Zhu Manhua, and the meaning of the words was very poignant. Unfortunately, when Mrs. Liu sang, the audience could only hear her voice and could not distinguish what words she was singing. This is probably because she has not received sufficient training in Chinese singing methods, and the movements of her mouth are not in accordance with the rules, so the pronunciation is not clear. As for the music of the song, perhaps it sounds very sad to Westerners, but to Chinese people, although it seems to be sad, it cannot evoke a lingering and weeping feeling. This is probably because Chinese and Western music have different reasons for expressing emotions!

After the singing, it was Afu's "Impression of Hutong in Beiping." In this song, the large tuning fork and gongs and cymbals used by barbers in the north were added to the Western string music and played together, which was very characteristic. It makes people feel a glimpse of life in the hutongs of Beiping from the music. When the performance ended, applause rang out, showing that the audience was very moved.

After the break, Mei Lanfang came on stage to introduce the play "Piano Heart Ripple," giving a brief speech, which was translated by a certain gentleman. Then the band began to play music, and the curtain was pulled open on both sides. The scenery was a palace and the shore of a lake, and the light and color were good. The most brilliant scene in the whole play was the fairy dance. The fairy was played by Ms. Yuan Meiyun, and her posture was very beautiful, her dance was extremely skilled, and she was in perfect harmony with the rhythm of the music, so when the dance ended, the audience applauded thunderously and were very satisfied. Among the other actors, the one who played the pianist was the best. The rest were also competent. The play is a pantomime, and all actions, words, and expressions are depicted with music, which is really not easy. Although we cannot say that this attempt is perfect, we are also very satisfied. This is a new path for Chinese old drama, and it has great potential for development. We hope that there will be opera attempts in the future, which will be a further step towards the improvement of Chinese old drama.

Film Reviews

Review of "Double Dealing" 283

— Zhong

In the past two years, Constance Bennett's productions have been numerous and of excellent quality, which is really surprising. Let's take a look at this "Double Dealing" (TWO AGAINST THE WORLD) shown by Cathay, which she performed for Warner Bros. She used to play the role of an innocent and lively girl on the screen, or a young woman in passionate love with a capable person, but her roundabout style remained, and she became a smart, capable, and sophisticated girl. It can be described as "the capable can do anything."

I think the story is a bit like "Tess of the Storm Country." Constance's performance also has similarities to Janet Gaynor's. Roughly speaking, the sister of a rich girl had an affair, and her brother obtained the evidence. In order to avoid the breakdown between her sister and brother-in-law, she took on the dishonorable matter herself. Her brother was furious and killed her sister's lover; she went to save him, but it was too late. The court thought that she committed the crime, and she was wronged even more. Fortunately, her brother realized his mistake and surrendered himself. A young lawyer intervened. She also explained the reason why her brother killed the man, and the judge thought that there was a reason for it and did not punish him. She then married the good lawyer.

Although there is a happy ending, except for the last

section, there is little talk of love; instead, there is a powerful depiction of family ethics. This is more desirable, but there are still three major loopholes:

First: the handbag that her brother used as evidence

, since it was her sister's thing, even though she admitted it, her brother-in-law did not doubt it at all. How could he not know anything about his wife's belongings and daily actions? Is he a fool? Second: her sister had improper behavior, but later she acted as if she was not involved, without any self-condemnation or sad reflection, which also feels unreasonable. Third: since she was willing to take the blame for others, she should have admitted to the murder. Seeing a lawyer and explaining everything was unnecessary. This contradicts her original will. There were also some loopholes added during the performance. For example, after the gunshot, the doorman did not immediately enter the room; these should be the responsibility of the director. There is also a big doubt: the evidence that her brother obtained was only a handbag, and he did not recognize that it was dishonorable and obscure. He was willing to die for the sake of his family's reputation, but it still feels like he was too nervous. Moreover, since he surrendered himself, the barrel of the pistol and the style of the bullet made it easy to determine the evidence of the murder with detective observation. Why was the judge helpless and had to wait for the girl's confession to be able to decide the case? The director also used extremely gorgeous costumes to show the wealth of the girl's family, but this was like an insult to a capable and virtuous girl. Not every rich girl is extravagant and lustful! The photography, lighting, and transitions are all good. The scenery is grand and beautiful. Warner Bros. invested a considerable amount of capital in this film. In other places, the director also worked hard, and the whole film is quite tense. Although there are shortcomings in the story, consciousness, and skills, the film is still transcendent. Constance's performance is profound, which she has not shown in the past. She gives the audience a lot of emotional stimulation. Neil Hamilton, who played the lawyer, tried his best to imitate a young man who was unclear, impetuous, and fond of winning, which was just right. Allen Vincent, who played the brother, was a little angry, but he was better in the second half. The sister and all the other actors were mediocre.

Review of "The Flag Lieutenant" 284

— Ling He

The British flagship held a dance party, and the heroes and beauties sang and danced, which was naturally a joyful and harmonious scene. There was a major named LTDICKY who kissed a general's daughter several times at that time, and their love words were lingering. Suddenly, he heard that the British fort was in urgent need and was surrounded by Arab people. The major and his close friend led troops to help. The major's friend volunteered to ask the flagship for help, but was injured by the enemy, so the major continued to go. When the reinforcements arrived, planes and cannons were mighty, and the Arabs were defeated. Afterwards, when rewards were given for meritorious service, the major attributed his great achievements to his friend, but in the end, rewards and punishments were clearly distinguished. In addition to receiving the reward, the major kissed the general's daughter again.

In this kind of story, what did the director do?

He used fragmentary short shots without large scenes. The war scenes were fake, there were only a very small number of frontal conflicts, and in some places, the war was simply treated as a child's play. Especially the noisy dialogue in the second half and the dull plot had a hypnotic effect. However, there were also a few beautiful shots, such as the flagship breaking through the vast sea at the beginning, especially when the army was concentrated at night, the clever lighting was really great. However, the director was ultimately a failure. There was nothing brilliant in the front, there was only one climax in the middle, but it passed by lightly.

Regarding the scenery, the fort was fake, which could be clearly seen. The devices in several parts of the flagship were repeated again and again. Other aspects were mediocre.

Regarding the actors, I don't think there is anyone who deserves

praise. Only the major's friend showed a loyal personality. The several female characters were not good. The comic characters were also unable to make people laugh.

Moreover, even in terms of the structure of the story, there are many problems. For example, the major's call for help was so coincidental. The major's refusal to accept the great achievements was also not very understandable.

In short, in any aspect, it is ordinary and there is no

distinctive feature, but it is not a complete failure.

Finally, let me talk about my personal feelings.

The translation name of "The Flag Lieutenant" is naturally very moving. If the content of the film grasped the heroic resistance of the weak nation and the victory in the extreme sacrifice, then this title would be appropriate. However, the content of "THE FLAG LIEUTENANT" is a blatant depiction of imperialism's invasion of colonies and the suppression of colonial resistance movements with all the most sophisticated weapons. When we see such a film at a time when armed soldiers are going deep into the territory and signing treaties under duress, who would not be heartbroken? After a massacre, the oppressors reward meritorious service and raise the cup of victory, but the invaded are lying dead. If the British flag that finally appeared on the screen was replaced with the Rising Sun flag, would we be able to calmly say that this aggressive war was indeed "The Flag Lieutenant"? Why not add a Chinese subtitle: "Long live imperialism"?

New Trend of Sound Cartoon Films 285

— Dong Lin

Adopting fairy tales as the theme and using five-color brilliance

Some people say: "Since the invention of sound movies

, this sound cartoon film has had the greatest success!" Although this sentence is a bit arbitrary, it is also very reasonable. I think everyone who has seen the sound cartoon film before the feature film must feel the same way! We can prove that this is true from the fact that many people go to see cartoon films specifically without bothering to see the feature films. The harmony between the black lines and the syllables is so beautiful and magical!

However, the themes of these sound cartoon films are often just those mice (MICKEY MOUSE). In addition, there has never been any new development, and in terms of content, it is gradually found that there is a shortage of resources. Then, if this continues, will it not lose its reputation? Under this situation, what has emerged is Walt Disney's "Silly Symphony." It is more meaningful to move fairy tales to sound cartoon films to replace the mouse films that are about to decline.

However, is it too difficult to express fairy tales that are rich in fantasy with only black lines in mouse films? Therefore, five-color brilliance has also been used. In the "Silly Symphony" that has been adopted; in "Pirates and Mermaids," "Toyland," and "The Witch's Forest," in the "Pirates and Mermaids," when the mermaid is swimming in the ocean, it is painted with colorful brilliance, which can really lead people into the illusion of the "Land of Fairy Tales." It is said that the results of the trial screenings of these three episodes are very promising.

In the near future, we movie fans in Shanghai

will also be able to see these new types of sound cartoon films. Our eyes are really blessed!

Publication of the "Spring Tide" Movie Script

The long-rumored "Heming" sound film "Spring Tide" has

been completed for a long time, and has now passed inspection. It is said that it will be released in Shanghai at the end of this month. The "Spring Tide" script has been published by the Film Culture Bookstore. The script is written in great detail and is a necessary reference book for those who study film and love Yunying. It also includes more than ten photos and is priced at one jiao. Those who state that this newspaper is introduced should send seven fen in stamps to P.O. Box 2119, Shanghai.

The Film Special Editorial Department

Movie Novel: Eternal Regret (THE WHITE SISTER (9)) 287

— Si Ping

Prince Charles Montede's face turned ashen, his brow furrowed in disappointment as he sat at his desk. He wondered what to do, but his heart had become a mass of sorrowful, dark, and chaotic emotions. He followed Mina's report that she had gone to the barracks. He immediately ordered the carriage to be prepared.

Although Angela arrived near the barracks, it was of no use. She couldn't get close to the gate. She shrank back at the sight of the sentries. Finally, she took a risk. She wrote a short note. The sentry promised to deliver it for her tomorrow. She got into the carriage and instructed the driver not to return to the palace, telling him to just drive, drive anywhere. She sat in the carriage, closed her eyes, and felt the carriage turning and winding along a long road from the barracks, and then slowly turning onto the main road. Suddenly, there was a violent collision. Everything went dark.

Angela slowly regained consciousness. She crawled out from under the carriage that had crashed into a ditch. A soldier ran to her side and asked if she was hurt. Her frightened eyes turned to a group of soldiers leaning over another wrecked carriage. Her frightened eyes recognized a strangely familiar carriage—her father's carriage!

'Is it him? Is it him?' Her lips and tongue were dry with horror.

'He is dead, Princess,' the soldier said quietly.

'Father!' she screamed. 'It can't be!' She wanted to rush to his side. But a kind shadow enveloped her. At this moment of crisis, Pastor Sala Sincere was her friend, her protector, her comforter.

The malicious people reveled in Prince Charles Montede's death, wagging their poisonous tongues. But Angela didn't care about the various rumors. The father who educated her and loved her, like a royal palace surrounded by high walls in a beautiful garden—her merciful father, on whom her whole being depended, had died a violent death, enough to make her wish she were dead. But remember, she must painfully remember in her heart that their last meeting was one of misunderstanding, staring angrily at each other—remember that he was chasing her, trying to rescue her from obscurity—remember that the carriage she was riding in that tragic night was the knife that killed her father—how could she forget this scene and this feeling?
